<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道令心離蓋趣愛言教有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、煩惱蓋離蓋趣愛言教。煩惱如同一個蓋子將內心的光明蓋住，有煩惱時心不能寂靜，一旦內心動盪不安，便不能見到諸法實相。因此佛開示弟子們要遠離煩惱，離開煩惱蓋。煩惱通常也是由邪知邪見來的，如六十二見趣等，不同的邪知見能引出許多的煩惱，以及三界愛的染污希求，故佛開示弟子們令心離蓋趣愛言教。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、五蓋離蓋趣愛言教。貪欲、瞋恚、昏沈睡眠、掉舉惡作、及疑是修止觀最初要遠離的，屬於較粗的五種煩惱，這五種煩惱也是一種蓋障。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無明蓋離蓋趣愛言教。無明是對三界的苦等不了解，這些也都是要遠離的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、隨釋3　戌一、初言教</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨著解釋，分三科；第一科初言教，說明最初言教的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，依為證得斷、離、滅界所有言說，是初言教。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最初的言教是聖正言教，其中說明聖人戒、定、慧、解脫、解脫知見，以令學習者能夠證得斷界（指初果）、離界（指初果以上乃至四果向）、滅界（證得有餘依滅、無餘依滅的境界），分為這三階段。斷界是斷三界分別起的煩惱，離欲的離界，滅界，指有餘依滅了則能成就無餘依涅槃的功德。這樣的言說是初言教，是佛開示的第一類聖正言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、第二言教</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二言教，說明第二言教的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依即於彼見勝功德，及於所治蓋處諸行深見過患所有言說，當知是名第二言教。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「彼」是指聖人的五分法身，行者聽到佛開示的五分法身，能見到殊勝的功德，也會想要成就聖人的功德。以及對於自己所對治的蓋障能夠的深刻見到許多的過患，不僅現在的色受想行識眼耳鼻舌身意有過患，未來也有過患，這樣的言說是厭離言教。指出行者應修四聖種，才能成就聖人的五分法身，因此佛開示厭離言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、第三言教</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三言教，說明令心離蓋去愛的言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨順如是緣性緣起所有言說，當知是名第三言教。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨順緣性緣起的所有言說，能斷無明，應知是名第三言教。其中，緣性是因緣、所緣緣、等無間緣、增上緣四緣，緣起是指十二緣起。當然緣起不離開緣性，緣性說的其實也是緣起。一切法都是由緣而起，有因有緣世間集，佛法說的就是緣起。如何不要有生死的緣起？則必須斷除無明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、總結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科總結，總體的結語。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6730"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是三種言教，總名毗鉢舍那支。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛在經中開示的三大類言教，總名為毗鉢舍那支：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種是開示聖正言教，聖人的功德。以大乘來說本論〈菩薩地〉卷38的〈菩提品〉、卷37的〈威力品〉，說明佛菩薩的功德，這一類是屬於聖正言教。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種是開示厭離言教，教導少欲喜足等所說二道資糧是屬於厭離言教。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種是令心離蓋言教，是說明斷除煩惱的言教，包括斷除一切煩惱、五蓋、無明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是三種修觀必須學習的言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、略攝要義3　午一、略標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝要義，要略歸納三種言說的要義，分三科；第一科略標列，要略標示列出三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此言教，以略言之，復有三種。一、能生樂欲言教，二、能正安處資糧言教，三、能正安處作意言教。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又，這些修毗鉢舍那的言教，要略可歸納成三類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能生樂欲言教。能令有情生起善法欲，好樂修行善法才能成就聖人的功德；相當於說明聖人功德殊勝的言教。如世間的商人要賺錢，會先說明所售商品可以治百病，可以令人得到什麼利益。佛說法也隨順世間人，先說明種種的功德，世人才會有欲望想要成就。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、能正安處資糧言教。修行要有前方便，在正式起修以前，生活起居也要配合修行。上座時修止觀，下座時也要保持正念正知，這樣才能互相資助。安處資糧即是成就果的因，必須積聚二道資糧，或四聖種，這類言教是屬於厭離言教。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、能正安處作意言教。提醒行者要如理作意，如修七作意。最少要得未到地定才名已得作意。可見修行要成功是要在內心之中如理作意才能成就的。指導以正見為先，如理作意的言教，名能令心離蓋趣愛言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、別配屬</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配屬，將二類三種言教各別配屬。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂聖正言教，名能生樂欲言教；厭離言教，名正安處資糧言教；令心離蓋趣愛言教，名正安處作意言教。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聖正言教，是能夠產生樂欲修行的言教；厭離言教，能使行者少欲喜足、樂斷樂修，如四聖種，或開示二道資糧等，也名正安處資糧言教；令心離蓋趣愛言教，由於修止修觀有五蓋的隨煩惱、六十二見趣及無明，因此需教導行者觀察緣起，修四念住、八正道等，這一些法門即是屬於令心離蓋趣愛言教，名正安處作意言教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋得名</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋得名，解釋這類言教攝屬於毗鉢舍那支。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此言教，勝奢摩他所攝受慧，名毗鉢舍那，是故說此言教名毗鉢舍那支。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止這三類言教，好樂聖道果，發起善法欲，積聚資糧，依所得定，於定中能如理作意修習觀行，成就無漏的聖道，此勝奢摩他所攝受慧，名毗鉢舍那，因此說這三類言教，名為毗鉢舍那支。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、無間殷重加行2　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無間殷重加行，修行人除了有正教授，勤求奢摩他、毗鉢舍那的教導，主要於實際行動時要沒有間斷的加行，而且要殷切慎重的加行才能夠有成就，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何無間、殷重加行？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是沒有間斷、很殷切、慎重的加行？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋2　午一、略標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科略標，約略的標出要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂常所作、委悉所作、勤精進住，當知即依止觀加行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　常所作是無間加行，指經常修習止觀。委悉所作是殷重加行，委是確實，悉是周備全部，指對於修止修觀能夠殷重詳細周備。行者若能夠勤精進住於常所作、委悉所作，應當了知即是指依止於止觀無間殷重加行</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6731"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、別廣2　未一、標列五種</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別廣，各別詳細說明勤精進的相貌，有五種精進，分二科；第一科標列五種，標示列出五種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="29469:68127"></a><a name="19782:68127"></a>又勤精進應知五種。一、被甲精進，二、加行精進，三、不下精進，四、無動精進，五、無喜足精進。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次勤精進應知有五種：被甲精進、加行精進、不下精進、無動精進、及無喜足精進。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋其漸次</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋其漸次，解釋精進的相貌及漸次。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中最初，當知發起猛利樂欲；次隨所欲，發起堅固勇悍方便；次為證得所受諸法，不自輕懱，亦無怯懼；次能堪忍寒熱等苦；後於下劣不生喜足，欣求後後轉勝轉妙諸功德住。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五種精進中，最初是被甲精進，猶如世間人需要先穿起盔甲，才去跟敵人打仗。被甲精進也是一樣，要先發起猛利的樂欲，形容行者有很強烈的歡喜心想要修止觀，知道人生無常，不知道明天先到還是下一生先到。常常有這種警覺性，心才會有猛利的樂欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種是加行精進，實際行動發起堅固勇悍方便，隨所歡喜的止觀加行，不怕辛苦，克服身體的種種障礙、不愉快的感覺，時間到就要去修行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種不下精進，是不怯弱害怕，不看不起自己，不認為自己不行，要想有為者亦若是。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四種無動精進，精進時要能堪忍寒熱、飢飽力劣等苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五種是無喜足精進，如果有一點點好的境界也不滿足，還要繼續精進。未圓滿前都必須精進，不會有少分的功德便喜足，認為這樣就夠了，必須追求後後更高的、展轉殊勝、展轉微妙的功德，欣求最圓滿的境界。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、出世間慧2　巳一、標證得</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科出世間慧，說明出世間慧的體相，分二科；第一科標證得，標示證得出世間慧。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由如是勤精進住，入諦現觀，證得諸聖出世間慧。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　清淨修止觀的行者，由於能夠安住在五種精進中修止修觀，而證入四諦的現觀，成就諸聖人出世間的智慧。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋為依2　午一、能除隨惑2　未一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋為依，解釋以無分別智為依，能除隨惑，能除我慢相貌，分二科；第一科能除隨惑，又分二科；第一科總標，整體標出要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於修道中，依止此慧若行、若住，能正除遣所依身中諸隨煩惱，令心清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者已證得無分別智，但是還沒有圓滿，必須要繼續修道。在修學聖道當中，依止無分別慧後所得後得智，平常行住坐臥或修止觀的時候，能夠正確排除遣離身心中的隨煩惱，令心清淨；證得諦現觀以後，還要繼續修道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、別釋2　申一、於行位2　酉一、釋2　戌一、思惟不淨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋於行位及住位的如理作意，分二科；第一科於行位，解釋於行位的如理作意，又分二科；第一科釋，解釋，又分二科；第一科思惟不淨，作意思惟不淨。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6732"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂住聚落、或聚落邊，若見少壯、端嚴、美妙形色母邑，即便作意思惟不淨，為欲損害緣彼貪故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初果聖人分別起的貪煩惱已斷除，還有俱生起的貪煩惱要斷除。聖人於平常生活中，住在村裡或聚落旁，出門時如果看到年輕貌美端正莊嚴的女子，即應作意思惟她是不淨的，身體裡面裝的是屎尿，這樣作意是為了要損害心中所緣的色貪。如果知道女子美麗的形相，都只是一層薄皮包著不淨物，一具流動廁所而已，應不會再生起貪心。聖人雖已證諦現觀也仍然要思惟不淨，修不淨觀，以斷除俱生起的貪瞋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、思惟慈相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科思惟慈相，為了對治瞋心，思惟慈相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若遇他人逼迫惱亂，即便作意思惟慈相，為欲損害緣彼瞋故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在修道位的時候若遇到眾生的逼迫、惱亂，使自己苦惱，混亂自己的精神，要作意思惟希望對方得到快樂，讓自己緣這類有情所產生的瞋心不要現起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是行時，能正除遣諸隨煩惱，令心清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者平常活動的時候，能夠有這樣的正見，正確的除遣貪瞋的諸隨煩惱，使令內心清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、於住位</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於住位，在修止觀時。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若遠離處，修習入出二種息念，除遣欲等諸惡尋思。如是住時，能正除遣諸隨煩惱，令心清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若在遠離聚落的地方，修出息入息二種數息觀，或者其它的五停心觀、四念處，此時內心若出現欲、恚、害、國土尋思、親里尋思、不死尋思、輕懱相應尋思、家勢相應尋思等各種惡尋思，必須立刻除遣。如是於寂靜處修止觀時如理作意，能正確除遣欲、恚、害等各種隨煩惱，使令內心清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、能除我慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能除我慢，能夠除去我慢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼依如是已所證得出世間慧，於一切行修無常想，能正蠲除所餘我慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類初果以上的聖人，雖然已證得出世間的無分別慧，然而於三界一切五蘊諸行還應思惟觀察修習無常想，依此無常想能斷除俱生起我慢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯五、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是善士為所依止，復得無倒教授前行，由此漸次能證有學圓滿解脫，得金剛喻三摩地故；亦證無學圓滿解脫，一切煩惱皆離繫故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是初果聖人善士，以所證出世間慧為所依止，於三種善友處獲得正確無顛倒的修習止觀的教授，又能夠無間殷重加行，於行位思惟不淨、思惟慈相，於住位調伏諸惡尋思、斷除我慢，這樣慢慢的能夠成就有學的圓滿解脫，得到金剛喻三摩地，以如同金剛一樣堅固的定力，斷除非想非非想處最微細的我執無明，證得無學的圓滿解脫，遠離三界一切分別起及俱生起的煩惱繫縛，壽盡時入無餘依涅槃的滅界，不受後有，永出三界，究竟解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6733"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、成解脫義2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科成解脫義，說明成就解脫的體相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何解脫？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是解脫？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、釋得名</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科釋得名，解釋得到解脫名的理由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂起畢竟斷對治故，一切煩惱品類麤重永息滅故，證得轉依，令諸煩惱決定究竟成不生法，是名解脫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者生起完全畢竟斷除煩惱的無分別智，將一切煩惱品類的麤重與種子永遠息滅，證得轉依，令諸煩惱決定究竟不再生起，成就盡智及無生智，是名解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、辨差別2　巳一、無所有處已離欲位</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨差別，辨明聖人斷煩惱的差別，分二科；第一科無所有處已離欲位，無所有處已離欲位能證得諸漏永盡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若聖弟子，無所有處已得離欲，唯餘非想非非想處所有諸行，復能安住勝有頂定，爾時無間能隨證得諸漏永盡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若聖弟子，三果聖人，於無所有處已得離欲，於此位中，唯有所餘非想非非想處受想行識的愛見慢無明未斷，又能夠安住在勝於有頂定的金剛喻定中，這時以此如金剛堅固的無所有處定為依，隨修無常、苦、空、無我其中一種觀行，能斷除非想非非想處最微細的俱生我執，無間證得諸漏永盡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、無所有處未離欲位</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無所有處未離欲位，說明於無所有處未離欲位的三果聖人斷煩惱的情形。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若所餘位，雖能漸斷彼彼諸漏，然非無間能隨證得諸漏永盡，如是乃至無所有處未得離欲。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是所餘於下地乃至無所有處尚未離欲的聖人，雖然能漸漸的斷除無所有處以下諸地的煩惱，然而不能無間隨順證得諸漏永盡，仍須相續無間、殷重精進修習止觀，直到將無所有處及非想非非想處的煩惱斷除，才能證得無學的圓滿解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第221頁：入處相應第41經；累計經數219經；大正藏（198）經<br />
　如是我聞：一時，佛住王舍城耆闍崛山。爾時、尊者羅睺羅往詣佛所，稽首佛足，退住一面。白佛言：「世尊？云何知、云何見，我內識身及外一切相，令我、我所、我慢，使、繫著不生」？爾時、世尊告羅睺羅：「善哉羅睺羅！能問如來甚深之義」。佛告羅睺羅：「眼若過去、若未來、若現在，若內、若外，若麤、若細，若好、若醜，若遠、若近，彼一切非我、非異我、不相在，如實知。耳、鼻、舌、身、意，亦復如是。羅睺羅！作如是知、如是見，我此識身及外一切相，令我、我所、我慢、使、繫著不生。羅睺羅！如是我、我所、我慢、使、繫著不生者，是名斷愛、轉結，正無間等，究竟苦邊」。佛說此經已，尊者羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這時佛住王舍城耆闍崛山，羅睺羅尊者向佛請法說：世尊，要怎麼樣了知，怎麼樣可以通達，不會執著內識身及外境，使令自己不執著內身為我、外境為我所，不再被種種的我慢及煩惱使繫著在三界中，這些煩惱現行及種子都不再生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛說：善哉，問得太好了！羅睺羅，你能請問如來甚深之義。佛開示羅睺羅：過去的眼、未來的眼、現在的眼，內身的眼或其他有情的眼，或麤指欲界的，細是指色界的，好是指美好的眼，或是醜陋的眼，或約時間而言，是久遠以前的、或是最近的眼，這一切的眼都不是我、也不是我所，也不是我在眼中、眼在我中，都不是這種情況，總之是無我的，你們應該要如實了知。以上是觀察眼的盡所有性，過去未來現在內外麤細好醜遠近，共十一個相貌；如所有性是觀察非我、非異我、不相在。如是在奢摩他中思惟眼耳鼻舌身意的盡所有性及如所有性，便可以斷除我見、我所見、我慢，成就阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是佛開示修無我觀的道理，無我觀成功了可以斷除三界愛、轉結，轉掉邪知邪見我見，能夠無間的證得解脫道。無間道也是無礙道、是正斷煩惱，於金剛喻定將三界一切愛見煩惱斷盡，無間隔而成就解脫道，所以等是指解脫道。究竟苦邊指成就阿羅漢果。佛開示後，尊者羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第222頁：入處相應第42~48經；累計經數220~226經；大正藏（）經<br />
　如內入處，如是外入處 ~ 色、聲、香、味、觸、法；眼識，耳、鼻、舌、身、意識；眼觸，耳、鼻、舌、身、意觸；眼觸生受，耳、鼻、舌、身、意觸生受；眼觸生想，耳、鼻、舌，身、意觸生想；眼觸生思，耳、鼻、舌、身、意觸生思；眼觸生愛，耳、鼻、舌、身、意觸生愛，亦如上說。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從41~ 48經，說及六根、六塵、六識、六觸、六受、六想、六思、六愛，等八類諸行，都可在奢摩他中觀修盡所有性及如所有性，斷除煩惱證得解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第222頁：入處相應第49經；累計經數227經；大正藏（199）經<br />
　如是我聞：一時，佛住王舍城迦蘭陀竹園。爾時、世尊告羅睺羅：「云何知、云何見，於此識身及外一切相，無有我、我所、我慢、使、繫著」？羅睺羅白佛言：「世尊是法根，法眼，法依，善哉世尊！當為諸比丘廣說此義。諸比丘聞已，當受奉行」。<br />
　佛告羅睺羅：「善哉諦聽，當為汝說。諸所有眼，若過去、若末來、若現在，若內、若外，若麤、若細，若好、若醜，若遠、若近，彼一切非我，非異我，不相在，如實正觀。羅睺羅！耳、鼻、舌、身、意，亦復如是。羅睺羅！如是知、如是見，我此識身及外一切相，我、我所、我慢、使、繫著不生。羅睺羅！如是比丘越於二，離諸相，寂滅、解脫。羅睺羅！如是比丘斷諸愛欲，轉去諸結，(正無間等，)究竟苦邊」。佛說此經已，羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　某一個時候在迦蘭陀竹園，佛開示羅睺羅：如何以智慧來通達，推求內識身、外六塵，都沒有我、我所及我慢、使、繫著。羅睺羅先讚嘆佛陀：世尊是正覺者，是證悟諸法實相的人，是法的眼，是法依，能夠斷眾生疑，是賢聖之所尊，應為比丘詳細說明此道理。比丘聽了以後可以信受奉行，修奢摩他毗鉢舍那。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛告羅睺羅如何作觀：觀眼的盡所有性，如實正觀眼耳鼻舌身意的盡所有性及如所有性，修無我觀。如是比丘超越我、我所，遠離我、我所相，寂滅、解脫。寂滅煩惱得解脫，轉去種種的煩惱，成就無間道及解脫道，這段文與前41經的文所說觀行是一樣的，只是說法的地點不同。　</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第223頁：入處相應第50~56經；累計經數經228 ~ 234；大正藏（）經<br />
　如內入，如是外入，乃至意觸因緣生受，亦如是廣說。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如49經所說在奢摩他中觀修內六入的盡所有性及如所有性，如是50-56經說及外六入、六識身、六觸身、六受身、六想身、六思身、六愛身等七類諸行，合有八種都是這樣修習無我觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第224頁：入處相應第57經；累計經數經235；大正藏（200）經<br />
　如是我聞：一時，佛住舍衛國祇樹給孤獨園。爾時、尊者羅睺羅往詣佛所，稽首佛足，退坐一面。白佛言：「善哉！世尊！為我說法！我聞法已，獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住。獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住已，如是思惟：所以族姓子剃除鬚髮，正信非家，出家學道，修持梵行，見法自知作證：我生已盡，梵行已立，所作已作，自知不受後有」。爾時、世尊觀察羅睺羅心，解脫慧未熟，未堪任受增上法。問羅睺羅言：「汝以授人五受蘊未」？羅睺羅白佛：「未也，世尊」！佛告羅睺羅：「汝當為人演說五受蘊」。<br />
　爾時、羅睺羅受佛教已，於異時為人演說五受蘊。說已，還詣佛所，稽首佛足，退住一面。白佛言：「世尊！我已為人說五受蘊，唯願世尊為我說法：我聞法已，獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住，乃至自知不受後有」。爾時、世尊復觀察羅睺羅心，解脫智未熟，不堪任受增上法。問羅睺羅言：「汝為人說六入處未」？羅睺羅白佛：「未也，世尊」！佛告羅睺羅：「汝當為人演說六入處」。<br />
　爾時、羅睺羅於異時，為人演說六入處。說六入處已，來詣佛所，稽首禮足，退住一面。白佛言：「世尊！我已為人演說六入處，唯願世尊為我說法！我聞法已，當獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住，乃至自知不受後有」。爾時、世尊觀察羅睺羅心，解脫智未熟，不堪任受增上法。問羅睺羅言：「汝已為人說尼陀那法未」？羅睺羅白佛言：「未也，世尊」！佛告羅睺羅：「汝當為人演說尼陀那法」。<br />
　爾時、羅睺羅於異時，為人廣說尼陀那法已，來詣佛所，稽首禮足，退住一面。白佛言：「世尊為我說法！我聞法已，獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住，乃至自知不受後有」。爾時，世尊 復觀察羅睺羅心，解脫智未熟，廣說乃至告羅睺羅言：「汝當於上所說諸法，獨於一靜處，專精思惟，觀察其義」。爾時、羅睺羅受佛教敕，如上所聞法、所說法，思惟稱量，觀察其義。作是念：此諸法，一切皆順趣涅槃，流注涅槃，浚輸涅槃。<br />
　爾時、羅睺羅往詣佛所，稽首禮足，退住一面。白佛言：「世尊！我已於如上所聞法、所說法，獨一靜處，思惟稱量，觀察其義。知此諸法，皆順趣涅槃，流注涅槃，浚輸涅槃」。爾時、世尊觀察羅睺羅心，解脫智熟，堪任受增上法。告羅睺羅言：「羅睺羅！一切無常。何等法無常？謂眼無常，若色、眼識、眼觸，如上無常廣說」。爾時、羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜隨喜，禮佛而退。 爾時、羅睺羅受佛教已，獨一靜處，專精思惟，不放逸住。所以族姓子剃除鬚髮，著袈裟衣，正信非家，出家學道，純修梵行，乃至見法，自知作證：我生已盡，梵行已立，所作已作，自知不受後有。成阿羅漢，心善解脫。佛說此經已，羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尊者羅睺羅去拜訪佛，希望佛為他開示佛法，然後精勤的修止觀，乃至證得阿羅漢果，他有這樣的願、有這樣的善法欲。但佛觀察羅睺羅的心，知道他的奢摩他、毗鉢舍那尚未成熟，沒有堪能性能受增上法，無法成就聖道的法，因此必須積聚足夠資糧。佛問羅睺羅說：你教導眾人五受蘊的道理了嗎？羅睺羅說：我還沒有為人說過此法。佛告羅睺羅：你應為人演說五受蘊。從這裡可以看到不一定證得聖道後才說法，雖然沒有證得聖道，為了令自己的善根成熟而說法，說法不是說給別人聽的，是不斷的勸告自己使令自己成熟聞慧，對於佛的言教能無倒受持。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　羅睺羅受佛教誨後，為眾人說五受蘊法，又回去拜訪佛，希望佛為他開示一個法門，讓他能夠專精思惟，乃至證得阿羅漢果。佛又觀察羅睺羅的心與解脫的智慧仍未成熟，無法成為法器，不堪受增上法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此，佛說：你應該為人演說六入處。羅睺羅，為眾人廣說六入處後，來到佛所，希望佛為他開示一個法門，讓他能夠專精思惟，乃至證得阿羅漢果。佛認為羅睺羅還是沒有成熟，所以繼續要他為眾人說法。羅睺羅又為眾人演說尼陀那（十二因緣法），羅睺羅說完因緣法，佛發現他還沒有成熟，又要羅睺羅去說了更多的法，這裡不再列出來。等到說完這些法以後，佛告訴羅睺羅，你應當對於上面所說的諸法，獨自在一靜處專精思惟觀察其義。羅睺羅思惟自己所聽到的法及為眾人說法以後，想一想這些法都是相通的，每一法與每一法都是互相隨順，而且都是趣向涅槃。這時佛認為他解脫的智慧已經成熟，堪任納受增上法。因此，開示他一切法無常。一切是指少分的一切。一切一切，則包括六根、六塵、六識、六觸、六受、六思、六愛，這些法都是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此時，羅睺羅受佛的教敕後，獨一靜處，專精思惟，安住於不放逸，乃至證得阿羅漢果。所以凡是佛的弟子，剃除鬚髮，著袈裟衣，正信非家，出家學道，純修梵行，乃至見法，自知作證：我生已盡，梵行已立，所作已作，自知不受後有，都能成就阿羅漢果，心善解脫。佛說此經已，羅睺羅聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　論主補充說：佛弟子為求於解脫，應如理聞思，久遠相續，令解脫的智慧成熟，成就有學解脫；有學解脫之後，久遠修道，令解脫的智慧更加成熟，而能成就無學解脫。又說行者修行要有五種多所作法：一、正教授。二、奢摩他支。三、毘缽舍那支。四、無間殷重加行。五、出世間慧。羅睺羅均一一奉行，因此能令心解脫，證阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑七、廣說煩惱16　寅一、三漏3　卯一、欲漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科廣說煩惱，此為「處擇攝」第一個總頌的第一個別頌（安立攝）中，第三句「解脫煩惱業」的「煩惱」，詳細說明煩惱，分十六科；將煩惱分成十六科詳說，第一科三漏，說明三種漏，欲漏、有漏、及無明漏，又分三科；第一科欲漏，說明欲漏的名義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5605:68157"></a><a name="73773:68157"></a>復次，諸欲界繫一切煩惱，唯除無明，說名欲漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，所有欲界的煩惱，除了無明不算在內，由欲引起的煩惱，名為欲漏。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6734"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、有漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有漏，說明色、無色界有漏的名義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸色無色二界所繫一切煩惱，唯除無明，說名有漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色界、無色界所繫縛的一切煩惱，除了無明不算在內，其它對於禪定的愛見慢疑煩惱等，名為有漏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、無明漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無明漏，說明無明漏的名義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸有情，或未離欲、或已離欲，除諸外道所有邪僻，分別愚癡所生惡見蔽覆其心；依此惡見，於彼諸欲一分尋求、一分離欲，乃至非想非非想處。於彼三界所有無智，總攝為一，立無明漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若諸有情，或未離欲，即欲界有情，唯除無明，欲界繫一切煩惱，名欲漏；或已離欲，即色、無色界有情，唯除無明，所有一切色、無色界煩惱，名有漏，這二類煩惱簡除了外道所有錯誤的邪僻分別，愚癡所生的惡見障覆其心，依此惡見，如五現法涅槃論者，一分主張於現在之五欲自恣受樂，故此欲界即為涅槃，因而尋求諸欲樂；另外四種主張色界初禪天、二禪天、三禪天、四禪天即為涅槃，因而追求離欲的色界定為究竟；乃至非有想非無想論者，由非有想非無想論門生起無明，執為解脫，而追求非想非非想處定。如是外道惡見於三界所有愚癡的無明漏，與以欲貪追求諸欲的欲漏，及有貪追求離欲的有漏定不同，此處追求三界欲是由「惡見」（思想）引生，這惡見引生的邪解脫欲，是一種無明漏，因此總攝為一種，安立為無明漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　簡而言之，外道於三界無智所生的惡見，攝屬於無明漏。如〈決擇‧聞所成慧地〉卷64說，略由五相，立邪解脫欲無明漏。一、有想論者，由有想論門生起無明；二、無想論者，由無想論門生起無明；三、非有想非無想論者，由非有想非無想論門生起無明；四、斷見論者，由斷見論門生起無明；五、現法涅槃論者，由現法涅槃論門生起無明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或未離欲或已離欲等者：前約欲界欲貪，說名欲漏。諸色無色二界有貪，說名有漏。今此總約三界無智，立無明漏。於三界中諸有情類，或未離欲、或已離欲，若為外道惡見所覆，依此惡見，於彼諸欲一分尋求、一分離欲，乃至非想非非想處，應知此非無明漏攝。如其次第，建立欲漏、有漏。前已說故，為簡別彼，是故除之。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文約欲界有欲貪，說名欲漏。色界、無色界有有貪，說名有漏。這裡是總約三界所有無智，即外道不知三界果報都是無常、苦、空、無我的道理，而安立無明漏。於三界中的有情，有一種是沒有離欲，或已離欲的有情，若為外道惡見所覆，依此惡見，於彼諸欲一分尋求、一分離欲，乃至非想非非想處，應知此是無明漏所攝（據卷64將外道惡見攝入無明漏，因此筆者此處解釋與韓居士不同）。如其次第，依貪煩惱已建立欲漏、有漏。前已說故，為簡別彼，因此將「惡見」癡煩惱簡除於欲漏、有漏之外，而安立為無明漏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、九結2　卯一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科九結，九種結縛，第一科總標，整體標出九結。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5316:68165"></a>復次，有九種事能和合故，當知建立九結差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有九種事能與苦和合在一起，而建立九結的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6735"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知建立九結差別者：此中九結，謂愛結、恚結、慢結、無明結、見結、取結、疑結、嫉結、慳結。如有尋有伺地說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#68167:5314">陵本八卷二頁544</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷8，224頁有提到愛結、恚結、慢結、無明結、見結、取結、疑結、嫉結、慳結，九結的名相，不過並沒有解釋九結的法相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別釋2　辰一、出九事</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別的解釋，分二科；第一科出九事，說出九種事。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何九事？一、依在家品，可愛有情、非有情數，一切境界貪愛纏事。二、即依此品，可惡有情、非有情數，一切境界瞋恚纏事。三、依有情數憍慢纏事。若四、五、六，依惡說法諸出家品，三種邪僻勝解纏事。謂依聽聞不正法故，依不如理邪思惟故，依非方便所攝修故，如是差別即為三種。七、於善說法律無勝解纏事。八、依出家品，智貧窮事。九、依在家品，財貧窮事。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪九種事？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、依在家品而立愛結，愛結是約在家人來說，在家人對於可愛的有情及非情物容易生起貪愛，如對人、動物、鑽石、古董、房子、車子等，因為愛著而有很多的苦惱出現。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、即依此在家品，對於厭惡的有情、非有情物有乖離愛，不想與之會遇、不想與苦受和合在一起，對此境界生起瞋恚的現行，是恚結。由於瞋恚而行不善，由此招未來生死之苦，被瞋恚所繫縛，流轉於三界而不能出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、依有情數憍慢纏事，是慢結。慢結主要是針對有情而起，依有情與別人比較而生出勝等劣種種的慢心出來。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、五、六，依惡說法諸出家品，而說三種邪僻勝解纏事，即：無明結、見結、及取結。第四種無明結，是外道出家人，由於聽聞不正法，由此遂招未來生死之苦，流轉三界，是名無明結。第五是見結、第六是取結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、見結，是外道出家人，依不如理邪思惟有我，而有斷常二見等邪見，因此安立見結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、取結，是外道出家人，依非方便所攝修，因修行的方便錯誤，而有欲取、見取、戒禁取及我語取等四取，依此安立為取結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、於善說法律無勝解纏事，立疑結。對佛說的法與律沒有殊勝的理解，心生疑惑，不能有決定的決擇智慧，依此安立為疑結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、依出家品，由智貧窮事，立嫉結。依出家人，因缺乏智慧而吝法，不能忍耐他人比自己有智慧，心生嫉妒，依此安立嫉結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、依在家品，由財貧窮事，立慳貧。依在家人，由於貧窮捨不得布施，依此安立慳結。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C89-02.htm">九結</a>）</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、配九結3　巳一、標如應</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配九結，依九事配九結，分三科；第一科標如應，標出如所相應的配屬。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此九事，如其所應，當知配屬愛等九結。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這九件事，如它所相應的，應當知道配屬於愛結、恚結、慢結、無明結、見結、取結、疑結、嫉結、慳結這九結。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋嫉結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋嫉結，特別解釋嫉結。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中由嫉變壞心故，於正法內發起法慳，由此當來智慧貧乏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛警誡弟子們，嫉妒破壞自己的內心，本應將自己所學的正法布施於請法者，於法慳吝不告訴他人，害怕他人的智慧強過自己，這種慳法的行為，於將來會感招智慧貧乏或愚癡的果報。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6736"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、指所餘</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三指所餘，指出所餘相應的八結。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘隨所應，配屬應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其餘的八種結，隨所相應，配屬應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、三縛2　卯一、辨因緣2　辰一、舉貪纏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科三縛，說明貪瞋癡三種繫縛，分二科；第一科辨因緣，辨別三種繫縛生起的因緣，分二科；第一科舉貪纏，舉出貪纏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，由為貪縛所纏縛故，於能隨順樂受境界，心不能捨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，由於被貪煩惱所纏繞束縛，心裡不能棄捨於各種能隨順生樂受的境界，如色聲香味觸法男女的欲界樂等，這是第一種纏縛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例瞋癡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例瞋癡，例說瞋癡的纏縛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是瞋縛所纏縛故，於能隨順苦受境界，心不能捨；由愚癡縛所纏縛故，於能隨順非苦樂受中庸境界，心不能捨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是被瞋煩惱所纏繞束縛的情形也是一樣的，心裡不能棄捨於各種隨順苦受的境界而生起的瞋，是瞋縛；由於被愚痴煩惱所纏繞束縛，對於各種能隨順生起非苦非樂受的境界，內心也是無法棄捨，這是癡縛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、結立縛</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結立縛，結說三縛的安立。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此因緣，故立三縛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這些因緣，是故佛安立三縛。貪瞋癡是有情經常生起的煩惱，具有繫縛的作用。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、七隨眠3　卯一、釋得名</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科七隨眠，說明七種隨眠，分三科；第一科釋得名，解釋得名的原因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5309:68184"></a>復次，煩惱品所有麤重隨附依身，說名隨眠。能為種子，生起一切煩惱纏故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱品類的所有麤重，麤重會使身心沒有堪能性、剛強不調柔性。麤重即是煩惱種子，煩惱還在種子的狀態，隨逐依附在身中，有能生起煩惱現行的功能，說名隨眠。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、明建立2　辰一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明建立，說明建立隨眠的原由，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出由二品差別建立七種隨眠。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46773:68186"></a>當知此復建立七種。由未離欲品差別故，由已離欲品差別故，由二俱品差別故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道佛有時又將煩惱歸納成七種。這七種隨眠，在〈本地分&bull;有尋有伺等三地〉卷8即有提及：「或分七種。謂七種隨眠，一、欲貪隨眠，二、瞋恚隨眠，三、有貪隨眠，四、慢隨眠、五、無明隨眠，六、見隨眠，七、疑隨眠。」由尚未離欲的有情品類差別安立欲貪、瞋恚二種隨眠；由已經離欲的品類差別安立有貪一種隨眠；由二俱品差別，即未離欲、已離欲的人都俱有的煩惱種子，安立慢、無明、見、疑四種隨眠，合計共有七種。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6737"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、別配</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配，將七種隨眠各別配屬未離欲、已離欲、或二俱的品類差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由未離欲品差別故，建立欲貪、瞋恚隨眠；由已離欲品差別故，建立有貪隨眠；由二俱品差別故，建立慢、無明、見、疑隨眠。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於未離欲，若遇可愛境便生貪，遇不如意境便生瞋，由此二種品類差別建立欲貪及瞋恚隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於已離欲，色界、無色界有情還是有愛著禪定的煩惱種子，故只建立有貪隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由未離欲、已離欲的人都俱有的煩惱種子，建立高慢心、無明、見、及疑四種隨眠。證得阿羅漢果才能盡除俱生我慢，禪定愈高慢心愈大；縱使已離欲得三界頂非想非非想處定者也還是有三界無明，所以未離欲及已離欲者都還有無明；見是指錯誤的邊執見及薩迦耶見，若未斷三界煩惱，還是有薩迦耶見乃至邊執見；未證聖道，都是有漏的境界，不論是已離欲或未離欲，對三寶、四聖諦都會有疑；所以慢、無明、見、疑這四種煩惱的種子通於未離欲及已離欲者皆具備。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結總攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結總攝，結說總攝。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是總攝一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是這樣安立七種隨眠，總攝含蓋了三界所有一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、隨煩惱3　卯一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科隨煩惱，說明隨煩惱，分三科；第一科總標，總相標出隨煩惱的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="49582:68193"></a><a name="64553:68193"></a>復次，隨煩惱者，謂貪不善根、瞋不善根、癡不善根，若忿、若恨，如是廣說諸雜穢事。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，隨煩惱有那些？包括貪不善根、瞋不善根、癡不善根，忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂等，如是詳細廣說所有的夾雜煩惱汙穢的事，都可以說是隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是廣說諸雜穢事者：如下別釋隨煩惱相，是名廣說應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下面解釋四十八種隨煩惱相貌，是名廣說應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別釋48　辰一、三不善根2　巳一、舉貪</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋隨煩惱，又分四十八科；第一科三不善根，解釋貪瞋癡三不善根的體相，又分二科；第一科舉貪，舉出貪不善根。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，能起一切不善法貪，名貪不善根。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道此隨煩惱中，凡是於可意境能生起一切不善法的貪煩惱，名為貪不善根，是不善的根本。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例餘</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘，例說其餘的瞋癡不善根。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瞋、癡亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　瞋不善根、癡不善根也是一樣。凡是於不可意境能生起一切不善法的瞋煩惱，名為瞋不善根；凡是於非可意非不可意境能生起一切不善法的無明煩惱，名為癡不善根。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6738"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、忿</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科忿，說明忿的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46789:68201"></a><a name="28842:68201"></a>若瞋恚纏，能令面貌慘裂奮發，說名為忿。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是瞋恚煩惱起現行，忿心一起，能令人咬牙切齒，面目猙獰，怒目橫眉，臉紅脖子粗，說名為忿。忿與憤義不同，憤以氣盈（怒氣充足）爲義，忿以狷急（性情躁急）爲義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、恨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科恨，說明恨的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">內懷怨結，故名為恨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　忿是瞋形於色，恨則是懷恨在心，沒有明顯的表相，恨與忿不並生，而是在忿之後生起。《阿毘達磨俱舍論》卷21：「恨，謂於忿所緣事中，數數尋思，結怨不捨。」即暴怒之後，不順心境界雖已過去，卻還懷念舊惡，恨意難消，故名為恨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、覆</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科覆，說明覆的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隱藏眾惡，故名為覆。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　覆，即是覆藏，或隱藏；隱藏自所作罪，故名為覆。為何須隱藏罪業？《成唯識論》卷6：「云何為覆？於自作罪恐失利譽，隱藏為性，能障不覆悔惱為業。謂覆罪者後必悔惱，不安隱故。」此即說明隱藏自罪的原因，即是「恐失利譽」，恐怕一旦自己罪行暴露，將會失去名聞利養。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、熱惱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科熱惱，說明熱惱的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">染汙驚惶，故名熱惱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心有煩惱，驚惶恐怖，身熱心惱，故名熱惱。《成唯識論》卷6：「云何為惱？忿恨為先，追觸暴熱，狠戾為性，能障不惱，蛆螫為業。」意即惱是在忿、恨之後所生的隨煩惱；此一煩惱是「追觸」所生，追念往惡（即恨），觸對逆緣（即忿），之後所生起驚惶恐怖，狠戾染污的內心狀態。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、嫉</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科嫉，說明嫉的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，不喜他榮，故名為嫉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有染污心，不能忍耐他人有光榮的事，不能隨喜，故名為嫉。《成唯識論》卷6：「云何為嫉？徇自名利，不耐他榮，妒忌為性。能障不嫉，憂慼為業。謂嫉妬者聞見他榮，深懷憂慼不安隱故。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰七、慳</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科慳，說明慳的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於資生具深懷鄙吝，故名為慳。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對日常所需的資生用品，心胸狹窄，吝惜錢財，不肯慷慨施捨，故名為慳。《成唯識論》卷6：「云何為慳？耽著財、法，不能惠捨，祕悋為性，能障不慳，鄙畜為業。」所以《法蘊足論》卷9說：「慳有二種：一、財慳；二、法慳。」此處論文只提及財慳。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6739"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰八、誑</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科誑，說明誑的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="4786:68214"></a>為欺罔彼，內懷異謀，外現別相，故名為誑。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為欺騙他人、令他迷罔，心裡懷著計謀，別有異圖，外表卻偽裝出另一副模樣，內濁外清，故名為誑。《大乘百法明門論解》卷2：「誑者，為獲利譽，矯現有德，詭詐為性」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰九、諂</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科諂，說明諂的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心不正直、不明、不顯，解行邪曲，故名為諂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諂媚是指為了取悅於人，便以不正直的言語去逢迎結好於對方。表面好像隨順他人，可是心裡是不正直的，不直接表達自己的想法，也不明顯告訴他人，心中的想法與表現的行為都是不正彎曲的，故名為諂。《大乘百法明門論解》卷2：「諂者，謂罔他故，矯設異儀，諂曲為性，能障不諂，教誨為業。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十、無慚</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科無慚，說明無慚的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所作罪，望己不羞，故名無慚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於自己所造的罪，一點也不覺得羞恥，名為無慚。《成唯識論》卷6：「云何無慚？不顧自法，輕拒賢善為性，能障礙慚，生長惡行為業。」無慚的特質是不顧自身與所受教法，心無羞恥。一個沒有羞恥心的人，既不尊重自己的人格，也不理會自己所受的戒定慧等教法，自暴自棄，自甘墮落。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十一、無愧</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科無愧，說明無愧的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所作罪，望他不恥，故名無愧。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對自己造的罪，相對望於他人，不覺得自己這樣有錯，故名無愧。《成唯識論》卷6：「云何無愧？不顧世間，崇重暴惡為性，能障礙愧，生長惡行為業。」無愧的特質是不理會世間輿論的力量，不怕愧對大家，也不以為作壞事是可恥的事。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十二、七慢7　巳一、慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科七慢，說明七慢，分七科；第一科慢，說明慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="34980:68222"></a>於他下劣謂己為勝，或復於等謂己為等，令心高舉，故名為慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　慢，又分二種情況：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、是與他人比較，若他人比自己差，便認為自己勝過他人，內懷高舉之心而藐視劣類，看不起德學比自己拙劣的人。即《俱舍論》所說的「於劣謂己勝」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、是他人與自己相等時，也認為自己與他人相等，而內懷高舉之心，不尊敬德學與自己同等的人。同《俱舍論》的「於等謂己等」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此種慢心，是依相較自己下劣、同等的二品有情而生起的。雖與實際情況相符，但其實與他人比較即有慢心出現。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、過慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科過慢，說明過慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於等謂勝，於勝謂等，令心高舉，故名過慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過慢，也分二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、是對依正二報的條件，或德學與自己同等的人，卻內懷高舉之心的硬說自己勝過對方。通於《俱舍論》說的「於等謂己勝」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、是他人勝過自己，卻偏說自己與他人相等，即《俱舍論》的「於勝謂己等」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此種慢心，是依與自己同等、勝過自己的有情而起，是超過事實的高慢心，故名過慢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、慢過慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科慢過慢，說明慢過慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6740"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於勝謂勝，令心高舉，名慢過慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於勝過自己的人，卻反過來說自己勝過對方，這種慢心比「過慢」更過頭，因此名慢過慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此種慢心，是依勝過自己的有情而起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、我慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科我慢，說明我慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">妄觀諸行為我、我所，令心高舉，故名我慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我慢是因虛妄的觀察而執著色受想行識是我、或我所；無論執著五蘊全部是我，或全部是我所，或五蘊其中的一蘊是我，另外四蘊是我所等，這些種種狀態的我執，都使令自心高舉，名為我慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我慢是七種慢的根本，因為眾生內執有我，故於他人起高慢之心，認為一切人皆不如我，乃至我所也比他人所有的都更高貴，這便是我慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此種慢心是依「我」而起，一切凡夫皆有我執，有我執者皆有我慢，只是有輕重的差別而已。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、增上慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五是增上慢，說明增上慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於其殊勝所證法中，未得謂得，令心高舉，名增上慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於殊勝的所證的聖道，自己沒有成就卻認為已經成就，未得謂得，令心高舉，名增上慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增上，有強盛之義，由於我慢未除，精進修行時，能得到一種相似的境界，因此生起高舉之心，謂我已證得聖果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此種慢心，可說是依「德」而起，行者因修行過程中稍有一點相應，生起高舉之心，錯誤的以為自己實有所證。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、下劣慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科下劣慢，說明下劣慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於多勝中，謂己少劣，令心高舉，名下劣慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他人勝過自己很多，但自認只輸一點點，令心高舉，是名下劣慢。有的地方也稱為卑慢、卑劣慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《百法明門論》中，卑劣慢又可分二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、是「自實甚劣，妄謂少劣」，同於此處所說，雖自他差距甚遠，但只承認自己不過是少分不如而已。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、是「雖知彼勝，不肯起敬」，雖完全承認他人程度比自己高強，但不肯虛心向對方學習，反而生起慢心的認為沒什麼了不起，也有這種情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、邪慢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七邪慢，說明邪慢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">實無其德，謂己有德，令心高舉，故名邪慢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　實在是沒有功德的惡行，卻以此仗恃，令心高舉，認為自己有功德，這種高慢心名邪慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有些惡人，坐牢犯法，不但不以為不名譽，反生高舉之心，認為坐牢次數越多越是好漢、殺人越多越是英雄等，這正是一種邪慢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上七慢，也可分為九慢，然而只要是慢，便是以生苦為業用，能障善法。因為一旦有慢心，便容易滿足現狀，不求上進，不能謙下，競生人我，由此輪轉生死無有窮盡，受諸苦惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十三、憍</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科憍，說明憍的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，隨恃榮譽形相疏誕，故名為憍。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憍與慢不同，慢為六根本煩惱之一，而憍為二十個小隨煩惱之一。什麼是憍？心懷染污的貪瞋癡，仗勢榮譽之境，作出一些不該作的事。譬如依恃父親有錢，十六七歲的人開著賓士汽車到處花天酒地，行為粗疏荒誕，表現超出應有的形相，名為憍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憍，有時也通作「驕」，即驕矜、放肆、自大自滿、恃才傲物之意。有驕之人，無有智慧，不論處在何種地位，都覺得高人一等。如《成唯識論》卷6六云：「云何為憍？於自盛事，深生染著，醉傲為性。」由此可知，自盛事是憍的所緣境。本論又歸納為：無病、少年、長壽、族姓、色力、富貴、多聞七種。又依《成唯識論》卷6所說，此是貪愛一分為體，離貪無別憍相用故。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十四、放逸</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科放逸，說明放逸的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸善品不樂勤修，於諸惡法心無防護，故名放逸。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於戒定慧、止觀、四念處等諸善品，不好樂精進修學，虛度時間，六根已經流出貪瞋癡慢疑等惡法，心不積極防守保護，任由煩惱馳騁，名為放逸。放縱自己的煩惱，放縱自己的身語意行為，這都是放逸。如《成唯識論》卷6云：「云何放逸？於染淨品，不能防修，縱蕩為性。」業用為「障不放逸，增惡損善所依為業。」屬於八個大隨煩惱之一。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6741"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十五、傲</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科傲，說明傲的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸尊重及以福田，心不謙敬，說名為傲。</span></strong></span></span>
