<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　高傲之人，對於所應尊重的父母、師長或是聖人這些福田，內心不能謙下恭敬，名為傲。通常由於自己有才華容易高傲，而對應尊重的福田不能謙下恭敬，如多讀了一點書就看不起自己的師父，這是有傲。如《法蘊足論》卷8云：「云何傲？謂有一類，應供養者而不供養，應恭敬者而不恭敬，應尊重者而不尊重，應讚嘆者而不讚嘆，應問訊者而不問訊，應禮拜者而不禮拜，應承迎者而不承迎，應請坐者而不請坐，應讓路者而不讓路；由此發生身不卑屈、不等卑屈、不極卑屈、身傲，心傲，自傲誕性，總名為傲。」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十六、憤發</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科憤發，說明憤發的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若煩惱纏，能令發起執持刀杖、鬥訟違諍，故名憤發。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱現行，能令當事者拿起刀杖、與人打鬥、爭訟、違抗、諍論，名為憤發。〈攝異門分〉卷84則說：「憤發者：謂出言顯發惡意樂故」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　另外，如前所說，忿與憤義有不同，憤以氣盈（怒氣充足）爲義，忿以狷急（性情躁急）爲義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十七、矯</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科矯，說明矯的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，為顯己德，假現威儀，故名為矯。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心有意圖，想要得到名聞利養，於是為了顯示自己的功德，假裝現出自己的威儀很寂靜，非常的有修行，名為矯。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　矯與諂有些相似，但諂是語業所表，矯則偏身業所現。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十八、詐</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十八科詐，欺詐，說明詐的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，為顯己德，或現親事、或行軟語，故名為詐。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心懷有染污、有貪瞋癡，為了顯示自己的功德，或現出親愛的事情、或說出柔軟語，話說得很好聽，但是別有意圖，名為詐。這是將身語二業合說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十九、現相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十九科現相，說明現相的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，欲有所求，矯示形儀，故名現相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心裡染污，想要有所求，於是假裝很有修行的外貌而穿破舊的衣服，讓施主以為自己有所匱乏，布施許多上妙的衣服等等，名現相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6742"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲有所求矯示形儀者：聲聞地說：又為貪求種種衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥資具因緣，方便顯己有勝功德，矯詐構集非常威儀。為誑他故，恆常詐現諸根無掉、諸根無動、諸根寂靜，由是令他謂其有德，當有所施、當有所作。所謂承事，供給衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥及諸資具。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/22.htm#68252:18887">陵本二十二卷十頁1919</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉說：為了貪求衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥資生具的因緣，而以種種方法顯示自己有殊勝的功德，矯詐的構畫、現出特殊的威儀。動機是為了欺騙他人，又常常假裝現出六根沒有掉動，非常寂靜，好似得定一般，使令他人認為自己有道德、修證有力，應該多布施，多為自己做事，包括所謂的供給衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥及諸資具。如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷22，800頁曾說的，它的義理應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十、研求</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十科研求，說明研求的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">現行遮逼，有所乞丐，故名研求。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現出行為以遮蔽內心的想法，但因實際有所期待，而苦苦的研磨逼求他人布施，故名研求。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷22所說：「或於淨信長者、居士、婆羅門所，如其所欲不得稱遂，或彼財物有所闕乏，求不得時，即便彊逼、研磨麤語，而苦求索。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十一、以利求利</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十一科以利求利，說明以利求利的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所得利不生喜足，悅獲他利更求勝利，是故說名以利求利。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於所得的衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥等，不能滿足，希望得到更多的利益，因此將施主布施的東西拿出來，以所得的利養再追求更多的利養，譬如告訴施主：「張三比你窮，但布施的卻比你還多，你應該要再布施多少。」這即是以利求利。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十二、不敬</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十二科不敬，說明不敬的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自現己德，遠離謙恭，於可尊重而不尊重，故名不敬。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不敬與傲有點不同。先自己顯現自己的功德，遠離謙恭的心行，而對於可尊重者不能尊重，故名不敬。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十三、惡說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十三科惡說，說明惡說的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於不順言性不堪忍，故名惡說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於想要反抗對方而說出不順對方心意的言語，名為惡說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於不順言性不堪忍者：謂不堪忍，發言麤獷故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指由於不能堪忍，說話麤獷，造惡口業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十四、惡友</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十四科惡友，說明惡友的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸有朋疇，引導令作非利益事，名為惡友。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類的朋友們，會引領誘導自己去作沒有利益的事，名為惡友。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6743"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十五、惡欲</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十五科惡欲，說明惡欲的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">耽著財利，顯不實德欲令他知，故名惡欲。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　耽著於自己的財富利養，也想從他人得到財利而顯現出不真實的功德，要令他人知道自己很有修行，名惡欲。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十六、大欲</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十六科大欲，說明大欲的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於大人所欲求廣大利養恭敬，故名大欲。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　希望從有功德、有福報、有富貴的人那裡，得到廣大的利養與恭敬，名大欲。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十七、自希欲</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十七科自希欲，說明自希欲的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">懷染汙心，顯不實德欲令他知，名自希欲。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　懷著不清淨心，顯現出不實的功德相，希求冀望他人知道自己很有德行、由此可以從他處得到名聞利養，名自希欲。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十八、不忍2　巳一、舉於罵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十八科不忍，說明不忍的體相，分二科；第一科舉於罵，舉出罵的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於罵反罵，名為不忍。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遭他人辱罵自己，反罵他人，這種人沒有忍耐性，名為不忍。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例於瞋等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於瞋等，例說於瞋等相貌</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於瞋反瞋、於打反打、於弄反弄，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他人對自己憤怒，自己也對他人起瞋、他人打自己，自己也要反打回去、他人不尊重自己，自己也找機會戲弄對方，以上是不忍的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二十九、耽嗜遍耽嗜2　巳一、舉於自他</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十九科耽嗜遍耽嗜，說明耽嗜遍耽嗜的體相，分二科；第一科舉於自他，舉出於自己及他人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於自諸欲深生貪愛，名為耽嗜。於他諸欲深生貪著，名遍耽嗜。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對自己已得到可意的色聲香味觸法，有很深的貪愛，名耽嗜。於自身以外有情可意的色聲香味觸法，也深深的耽著，名遍耽嗜。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例於勝劣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於勝劣，例說於勝於劣都耽嗜</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6744"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於勝於劣，隨其所應，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於殊勝的色聲香味觸，心生貪著，如喜歡鑽石是耽嗜，連較低劣的人工鑽石、玻璃製品等也貪著，是遍耽嗜。隨其所相應的事物，不論是勝是劣都喜歡，也是如此。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十、貪</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十科貪，說明貪的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸境界深起耽著，說名為貪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於種種色聲香味觸男女，欲界的境界，深深的生起愛著，名貪。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十一、非法貪</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十一科非法貪，說明非法貪的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="34941:68283"></a>於諸惡行深生耽著，名非法貪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於犯法惡事耽著不捨，如世間人知道吸毒不好，可是沉溺其中不能自拔，名非法貪。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十二、執著</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十二科執著，說明執著的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於自父母等諸財寶不正受用，名為執著。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對自己的父母、親人的錢財寶物，執為己有，任意受用，名為執著。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十三、惡貪</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十三科惡貪，說明惡貪的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於他委寄所有財物規欲抵拒，故名惡貪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於他人委託寄存的財物起貪心，拒還他人，占為己有，故名惡貪。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十四、見有見無有見</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十四科見有見無有見，說明我見、常見、斷見體相</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="67735:68289"></a>妄觀諸行為我、我所，或分別起、或是俱生，說名為見。薩迦耶見為所依止，於諸行中發起常見，名為有見。發起斷見，名無有見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　虛妄的觀察五蘊諸行，執著色受想行識是我、或是我所，或是透過學習分別起的我見，或是與生俱來俱生的我見，說名為見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於自身色受想行識上生起我、我所見，名薩迦耶見。以薩迦耶見為所依止，於五蘊之身，妄計為常，認為今世雖滅，後世復生，相續不斷，是名有見。有見也就是常見。若妄計今世滅已，更不再生，則成斷滅，是斷見，名無有見，例如人死如燈滅，滅了就沒有了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十五、五蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十五科五蓋，說明五蓋的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6745"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知五蓋，如前定地已說其相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道五蓋是修止觀時最容易現前的五種煩惱，在本論〈三摩呬多地〉卷11中已經說過五蓋的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、貪欲蓋。「貪欲者，謂於妙五欲隨逐淨相，欲見、欲聞，乃至欲觸；或隨憶念先所領受，尋伺追戀。」於微妙的色聲香味觸法五欲，生起淨妙想，隨逐五欲境界而轉，而想去見聞、乃至想接觸，或於靜坐時隨順憶念過去曾領受過的微妙五欲，不斷尋伺回想追求迷戀，忘失所緣境，障礙得定。對現前欲境的取著及過去欲境尋伺憶念的種種心相，名為貪欲蓋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、瞋恚蓋。「瞋恚者，謂或因同梵行等舉其所犯，或因憶念昔所曾經不饒益事瞋恚之相，心生恚怒；或欲當作不饒益事，於當所為瞋恚之相多隨尋伺，心生恚怒。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　瞋是瞋心，是根本煩惱；恚是隨煩惱，隨逐瞋心而生起憤怒的相貌。瞋恚有三種情況：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、因同梵行等舉其所犯：在一起共同修學聖道的人舉發自己過失，心裡忿恨不平。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、或因憶念昔所曾經不饒益事瞋恚之相，心生恚怒：或者因為回憶過去曾接觸過的一些不愉快之事，心生瞋惱恨恚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、或欲當作不饒益事，於當所為瞋恚之相多隨尋伺，心生恚怒：或想要報復作對他人不利的事，內心生起瞋惱恨恚。以上三種瞋恚相，修止觀時令心多隨尋伺，尋求作惡方便，不斷的分別，心生恚怒，障礙得定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以此瞋恚，蓋覆心識，禪定、善法不能發起 沈淪三界，不能出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、惛沈睡眠蓋。惛沈的七種原因：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、或因毀壞淨尸羅等隨一善行。戒持不清淨，又沒有懺悔，打坐便容易惛沈。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、不守根門。六根攀緣六塵，貪好色聲香味觸法的境界，不能密護根門容易惛沈。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、食不知量。吃太多，或吃太少，都是惛沈的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4、不勤精進，減省睡眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5、不正知住而有所作，不能正確的知道自己現在的身語意是什麼狀態，容易惛沈。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　6、於所修斷不勤加行。由於不常精進地修止觀，不數數練習，也容易惛沈，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　7、隨順生起一切煩惱，令身心惛昧，無堪任性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　睡眠者；謂心極昧略。睡眠是心非常的暗昧，沒有力量可以緣所緣境。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼惛沈及睡眠會合成一蓋？睡眠以惛沈為緣，它是最接近惛沈的心所法。所以說：無餘近緣如睡眠者。也就是惛沈的時候，必定會睡眠，因此合立成一蓋，稱為惛沈睡眠蓋。由此障礙修習止觀、覆蓋所緣境相，使行者不能得禪定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、掉舉惡作蓋。掉舉，是指因掉動而高舉，令心浮動不安，障礙修止。通常因為親屬之間的親情、憶念家鄉國土的種種往事、或者不能了知人命無常、或憶念過去所經歷過的，戲笑歡娛時所行之事，令心不寂靜，躁動不安，障礙止觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惡作是對於過去所做的事情，或沒有做的事情，心中追憶後悔。例如後悔當初離開父母親屬，離開家鄉或自己熟悉的地方 或是應該作的沒有作、不應該作的又作了，心生後悔名為惡作，這種後悔的心情不能棄捨，讓心裡動盪不安。由此障礙修習止觀、覆蓋所緣境相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　掉舉與惡作憶念的所缘境相同，掉舉有親屬尋思、國土尋思、不死尋思，或隨憶念昔所經歷戲笑歡娛所行之事，令心不寂靜，惡作也是一樣，所以合說一蓋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以此掉舉惡作，蓋覆心識，禪定、善法不能發起 流轉三界，不能出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、疑蓋，對於師長、佛法僧、所學的教法、或師長的教導、或於所證的世間出世間的功德，有迷惑，不完全明白，修止觀時，懷疑三寶、三學、涅槃及自己的能力。又對於過去、未來、現在到底有沒有我？及於苦集滅道四諦，心生迷惑懷疑。心懷二分，心中有二種想法，是有？還是沒有？心裡迷惑不明、猜測揣度，不能決定。這是疑蓋，也會障礙行者得到禪定及聖道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如前定地已說其相者：謂如三摩呬多地說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/11.htm#68293:8285">陵本十一卷三頁845</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如〈三摩呬多地〉卷11，352頁所說五蓋應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十六、𧄼瞢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十六科𧄼瞢，𧄼瞢（音：ㄊㄥˊ，ㄇㄥˊ，目暗、目不明義）。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不如所欲，非時睡纏之所隨縛，故名𧄼瞢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修學止觀並不是睡覺的時候，但這時睡眠煩惱生起，不如自己所期待的勤進在所緣境上，這種狀態，名為𧄼瞢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十七、不樂</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十七科不樂，說明不樂的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非處思慕，說名不樂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不合道理的思惟羡慕，如：行者不歡喜現在修行的狀態，希望去受用欲樂的境界，心就不快樂，此非處思慕，名為不樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十八、頻申</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十八科頻申，說明頻申的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">麤重剛彊，心不調柔，舉身舒布，故曰頻申。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身體麤重沒有堪能性，彊硬、剛強不調柔，於是將整個身體舒張起來，這樣的威儀，代表內心有煩惱，心不調柔，此伸懶腰的身相，名為頻申。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三十九、食不知量</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三十九科食不知量，說明食不知量的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所飲食不善通達若過、若減，是故名為食不知量。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於所受用的飲食不能善巧的通達是不是過量，或不足。食用不夠，沒有力氣，食用太多易昏沈，遇到美味便吃太多，不好吃又吃過少，此食不知量也是一種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十、不作意</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十科不作意，說明不作意的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所應作而便不作，非所應作而更反作，如所聞思修習法中，放逸為先，不起功用，名不作意。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　出家卻遠離所生善法，應該作的事不去作，不應作的事反而去作。如所聽聞思惟的佛法，於善法不能精進，於惡法不能防護，因此不能讓修行得到一個好的結果，名不作意。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6746"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十一、不應理轉</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十一科不應理轉，說明不應理轉的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所緣境深生繫縛，猶如美睡隱翳其心，是故說名不應理轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修止觀時由於所緣境令心得到輕安，因此深生愛著，繫縛於此，好像美睡眠隱藏障覆自己的覺心，不能進一步修習聖道破除定愛，名為不應理轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十二、心下劣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十二科心下劣，說明心下劣的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自輕懱故，名心下劣。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自己看不起自己，對於殊勝之事，成佛的事如修行都還沒去實踐，馬上生起放棄的念頭，名為心下劣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十三、抵突</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十三科抵突，說明抵突的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為性惱他，故名抵突。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類有情生性喜歡以身業或語業去觸犯逼惱他人，名為抵突。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十四、諀訾</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十四科諀訾，說明諀訾的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">性好譏嫌，故名諀訾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類有情生性喜歡譏笑嫌棄毀謗他人，名為諀訾。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十五、不純直</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十五科不純直，說明不純直的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欺誑師長、尊重福田及同法者，名不純直。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於師長、三寶、父母這些福田，及對一起修行的同法者，以欺誑的心，用種種的方法蒙蔽他們，名不純直。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十六、不和軟</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十六科不和軟，說明不和軟的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身語二業皆悉高疏，其心剛勁，又不清潔，名不和軟。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身業及語業姿態驕慢高傲，不可一世，內心剛強，不容易接納別人的勸諫，堅持自己的思想，心有染污不清淨，不能與他人和合，名不和軟。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十七、不隨順同分而轉</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十七科不隨順同分而轉，說明不隨順同分而轉的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6747"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸戒、見、軌則、正命皆不同分，名不隨順同分而轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本來僧團同住應該要戒和同修，見和同解，利和同均，意和同悅，身和同住，口和無諍，所有軌則都要共同遵守，生活所需來源要正確，反之與同梵行者不能修六和敬，這是一種煩惱的相貌，名不隨順同分而轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四十八、八尋思8　巳一、欲尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四十八科八尋思，說明八種尋思的體相，分八科；第一科欲尋思，說明欲尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="70251:68321"></a><a name="69820:68321"></a><a name="32358:68321"></a><a name="32244:68321"></a><a name="14787:68321"></a><a name="10919:68321"></a><a name="8444:68321"></a>心懷愛染，攀緣諸欲，起發意言，隨順隨轉，名欲尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心中懷著貪愛的染污，攀緣色聲香味觸法男女諸欲的境界，起發第六意識的意言，隨順諸欲引發內心種種尋思，名欲尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨順隨轉者：引發令生，是名隨順。生已相續，是名隨轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心愛著欲，攀緣五欲的境界而引發種種欲的尋思，是名隨順。欲生起時，心隨著五欲相續活動，不能停止下來，是名隨轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、恚尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二是恚尋思，說明恚尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷憎惡，於他攀緣不饒益相，起發意言，隨順隨轉，名恚尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心含藏憎惡之想，於其他有情攀緣生起不利於他人的想法，起發第六意識的意言，隨順不饒益相相續思惟不能止息，名恚尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、害尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科害尋思，說明害尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷損惱，於他攀緣惱亂之相，起發意言，餘如前說，名害尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心含藏損害、惱怒的想法，於他人攀緣生起惱亂他人之想，起發第六意識的意言，隨順損惱之想，這種煩惱名害尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、親里尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科親里尋思，說明親里尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，攀緣親戚，起發意言，餘如前說，是故說名親里尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心含藏種種染汙的想法，攀緣父母兄弟姊妹親友，起發第六意識的意言，隨順親里尋思的想法，相續不捨，這種煩惱名親里尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、國土尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科國土尋思，說明國土尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，攀緣國土，起發意言，餘如前說，是故說名國土尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心含藏貪瞋癡的染污，攀緣不同國土的美好境相，起發第六意識的意言，隨順國土尋思的想法相續不捨，這種煩惱名國土尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、不死尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不死尋思，說明不死尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6748"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="16949:68333"></a><a name="8451:68333"></a>心懷染汙，攀緣自義，推託遷延，後時望得，起發意言，餘如前說，是故說名不死尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心懷著染污的想法，攀緣對自己有利益的事情，如修習戒定慧等事，推託遷延，不肯及時行道，希望以後再作，生起發動第六意言，由此意識在心中隨順染污的想法作各種不死的尋思，名為不死尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、輕懱相應尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科輕懱相應尋思，有高慢心才會輕懱，與他人比較會有這種尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，攀緣自他若劣若勝，起發意言，餘如前說，是名輕懱相應尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心懷著染污的想法，攀緣自己或他人的興盛之事，生起若劣若勝的比較之心，起發第六意識的意言，相續不斷，是名輕懱相應尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、家勢相應尋思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科家勢相應尋思，說明家勢相應尋思的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心懷染汙，攀緣施主往還家勢，起發意言，隨順隨轉，是名家勢相應尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心懷著染污的想法，攀緣施主往還有財勢的施主家，生起發動第六意言，由此意識在心中隨順染污的想法，名為家勢相應尋思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、指餘</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科指餘，指出上列四十八種以外的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">愁、歎等事，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愁歎苦憂惱等事也是屬於隨煩惱，如前面〈攝事分〉卷88所說：「由可愛事無常轉變，悲傷心慼，故名為愁。由彼發言咨嗟歔欷，故名為歎。因此拊膺，故名為苦。內懷冤結，故名為憂。因茲迷亂，故名為惱。」應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於可愛的事發生無常轉變，心情悲傷憂慼，鬱鬱不樂，故名為愁；由於心情愁傷低落而發出嘆息抽噎的言語，為什麼是這樣？為什麼生病的是我？這是感歎的煩惱。愁歎至極，因此用手捶打自己的胸膛，哀痛欲絕，整個人都不舒服，是一種煩惱苦。內心懷冤抱屈，不能接受此無常轉變，心不舒暢，故名為憂。若又因此而迷惑障亂，過了半月、一年、十年，心都不曾平靜便是惱，憂的延長即是惱。這些都是隨煩惱的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》愁歎等事如前應知者：謂如前說愁、歎、苦、憂、惱諸相差別應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/88.htm#68340:67155">陵本八十八卷三頁6644</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前〈攝事分〉卷88，2615頁所說的愁、歎、苦、憂、惱各種相狀差別應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、纏2　卯一、標一切</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科纏，煩惱數起現行名纏，分二科；第一科標一切，標出一切。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，一切煩惱皆有其纏，由現行者悉名纏故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，所有的煩惱都有生起現行的可能性，由於煩惱現行如繩索纏縛著身心，故名為纏。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8：「數起現行，故名為纏」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋建立2　辰一、標唯八種</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋建立，解釋纏的建立，分二科；第一科標唯八種，標出只有八種纏。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6749"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">然有八種諸隨煩惱，於四時中數數現行，是故唯立八種為纏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然廣說所有的煩惱現行都名為纏，然而有八種隨煩惱，特別在修學戒、定、慧與受用財法這四種時中時常起現行，因而此處只安立八種隨煩惱的現行為纏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋於四時4　巳一、於修學戒時</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋於四時，解釋四時的內容，分四科；第一科於修學戒時，於修學持戒時，有無慚無愧這二種煩惱，能障礙持戒清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於修學增上戒時，無慚、無愧數數現行，能為障礙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一時是指於修學增上戒時，有無慚、無愧二種隨煩惱常常起現行，能為行者持戒清淨的障礙。前文說無慚是「於所作罪，望己不羞」；無愧是「於所作罪，望他不恥」。若常常不自重，也不覺犯錯是愧對師長與聖賢，便容易不尊重戒法而放縱身口犯戒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、於修學心時</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於修學心時，在修學增上心（修定）時，有惛沈、睡眠這二種煩惱，能為障礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於修學增上心時，惛沈、睡眠數數現行，能為障礙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二時是指於修學增上心時，有惛沉、睡眠二種隨煩惱常常起現行，能為行者修定的障礙。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11說：「順生煩惱、壞斷加行，是惛沈性；心極昧略，是睡眠性。又惛昧無堪任性，名惛沈；惛昧心極略性，名睡眠。」總之，惛沉睡眠使身心惛昧，無堪任性，無法將心安住於一個所緣境上，數數憶念，不堪修止。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、於修學慧時</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科於修學慧時，於修學觀慧時，有掉舉、惡作這二種煩惱，能為障礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於修學增上慧時，簡擇法故，掉舉、惡作數數現行，能為障礙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三時是指於修學增上慧，必須思維簡擇法義時，有掉舉、惡作二種隨煩惱常常起現行，能為行者修學觀慧的障礙。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11說：「掉舉者，謂因親屬尋思、國土尋思、不死尋思，或隨憶念昔所經歷戲笑歡娛所行之事，心生諠動騰躍之性。惡作者，謂因尋思親屬等故，心生追悔&hellip;或因追念昔所曾經戲笑等事，便生悔恨&hellip;由如是等種種因緣，生憂戀心，惡作追悔。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在修毘鉢舍那時，本來應該是觀想無常苦空無我等法義，卻因掉舉惡作而使心攀緣至世間法去了，掉舉惡作若數數現行能障礙修觀，無法修學增上慧。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、於受用財法時</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科於受用財法時，於受用財法時，有嫉妒、慳吝這二種煩惱，能為障礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若同法者展轉受用財及法時，嫉妒、慳吝數數現行，能為障礙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四時是指若同梵行者於受用財及法時，有嫉妒、慳吝二種隨煩惱常常起現行，能為行者修學的障礙。大家一起共同修學，本應是利和同均，共同受用施主供養的衣食湯藥與受用同一法味。若受用財或法時，認為他人的勝過自己，便生起嫉妒的煩惱，不耐他榮；或心胸狹窄，耽著財、法，不能惠捨共享於大眾，這是慳吝；此二隨煩惱能障礙不嫉與不慳，以生出憂慼與蓄積為業用。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、四暴流2　卯一、約界繫辨2　辰一、舉欲暴流</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科四暴流，說明四種暴流，暴流也是煩惱的異名，〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8說：「深難渡故，順流漂故，名暴流」，煩惱能使善品流失，猶如洪水使家屋樹木流失，分二科；第一科約界繫辨，約界繫分別，又分二科；第一科舉欲暴流，舉出欲界暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，欲貪瞋等欲界所繫煩惱行者，欲界所繫上品煩惱未斷、未知，名欲暴流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有貪瞋等欲界所繫煩惱的行者，若欲界所繫縛的上品粗重煩惱，還未斷除，也不了解，不知道這是煩惱，是屬於欲暴流。未斷未知故，將不斷的被這些煩惱所沈漂或淹沒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例餘隨應</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘隨應，例說其餘三種暴流所相應的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6750"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有、見、無明三種暴流，如其所應，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有暴流、見暴流、無明暴流三種，如其所相應的煩惱，應當了知也是如此。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有暴流是指色、無色界的煩惱，這一類愛見慢疑煩惱屬於有覆無記，會障礙得聖道，使令有情仍在生死中流轉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見暴流是指薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見等，錯誤的知見也像暴流一樣深廣難渡，甚難出離。凡夫常被見暴流所淹沒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明暴流是指對三界的無知，與癡相應之煩惱，不知我空、法空的真理，這也是一種很大的暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、約補特伽羅辨2　辰一、除外道攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約補特伽羅辨，約人來分別四種暴流，分二科；第一科除外道攝，除了外道所攝。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於欲界未得離欲，除諸外道，名欲暴流。已得離欲，名有暴流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在欲界還未離欲的人，除了諸外道之外，都繫屬於欲暴流。其實外道四種暴流都有，並不是說外道沒有欲暴流，而是說這種煩惱很普遍，只要是未離欲的人都有欲暴流。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修世間禪定已離欲得到色無色界定的人，還是有色無色界定愛，這些愛見慢無明煩惱，是屬於有暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、諸外道攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科諸外道攝，外道所攝的是見及無明這二種暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸外道，從多論門，當知有餘二種暴流。謂諸惡見略攝為一，名見暴流；惡見因緣略攝為一，說名第四無明暴流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸外道也有欲暴流、有暴流，然而約著外道最根本的煩惱是在思想上的錯誤，從多門外道論來看，應當知道外道還有其餘見與無明二種暴流。惡見是以薩迦耶見為根本，所引生出的六十二種邪見，略攝為一，名見暴流。約著產生邪見的因緣略攝為一，主要是指無明，不了解三界的色受想行識都是無我的道理，因而安立第四種無明暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、軛</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科軛，前面〈攝異門分〉卷84說煩惱能為現法生死流轉的最大方便，故煩惱也稱作軛，因為它能繫縛有情久溺於生死洪流中，猶如牛馬頸背受軛木扼住而挽車，不得自在。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若諸煩惱等分行者，非增非減，即上所說一切煩惱，說名為軛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，《雜集論》卷13說：「等分行補特伽羅者：謂住自性位煩惱。遠離猛劣，住平等位諸煩惱故。隨境界勢力，煩惱現行故。」這類人雖每種煩惱勢力都平等，無有特別強大或特別羸弱的煩惱，但因以上所說的一切五十三種煩惱都具足，如同被木軛緊緊套住，在三界中不得自在，故說名為軛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅九、四取2　卯一、略顯</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科四取，取是煩惱的別名，有執取、執持二義，又可分為欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取四種，分二科；第一科略顯，要略顯示四取的建立。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="7122:68366"></a>復次，當知依於二品建立四取。一、在家品，二、外道法中諸出家品。當知此中，若所取、若能取、若所為取，如是一切總說為取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當知道依於二種品類有情各別出現的煩惱，而安立四種取。一、在家人，二、外道法中的出家品。應當知道此四取中，有所取著的境界、能取著的心、取著的原因，如是一切總說為取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣釋2　辰一、取行相3　巳一、所取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣釋，詳細解釋，分二科；第一科取行相，說明取的行相，又分三科；第一科所取，說明所取的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何所取？答：欲、見、戒禁、我語是所取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是所取的境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：欲、見、戒禁、我語這四種都是所取著的緣境；所取的欲如色聲香味觸男女；所取的見，如薩迦耶見、邊執見等；所取的戒禁是指由邪見而執著受持的身語行為之戒禁；所取的我語是指世人所執著的我、我所，這些都是取的所緣境。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6751"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、能取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能取，說明能取的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="71313:68371"></a>問：何能取？答：四種欲貪是能取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是能取？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：四種欲貪是能取。對欲有欲貪是欲取，對見有欲貪是見取，對戒禁有欲貪是戒禁取，對我執有欲貪是我語取。能取的心，包括這四種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、所為取2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科所為取，說明所為取的體相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何所為取？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼要取著？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答4　未一、為得欲等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分四科；第一科為得欲等，說明為得到諸欲而有欲取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：為得諸欲及為受用故，起初取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依在家人說，在家人一定是生活在欲當中，為得到諸欲的滿足以及為了受用飲食男女等諸欲的緣故，而生起第一種取，即欲取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、為詰他等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為二科為詰他等，說明為了詰責他所立論或免脫他人的問難等，而有見取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由貪利養及以恭敬增上力故，或為詰責他所立論，或為免脫他所徵難，起第二取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道的出家人由於貪著名聞利養及他人對自己的恭敬，這份增上力的緣故，便致力於以擊敗他人論點來破他立自，或為了免脫他人的難問，而成立自己的理論，因此生起第二種取，即見取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、為趣離欲</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為趣離欲，外道為了離欲得定，而有戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">奢摩他支為所依止、為所建立，為欲往趣世間離欲乃至非想非非想處三摩鉢底，起第三取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道以奢摩他支為所依止、為所要建立的禪定，為了得到世間離欲，初禪、二禪、三禪、四禪乃至非想非非想處的等至，錯誤的取著種種身語的禁戒，以作為入定必須的條件，因而生起第三種取，即戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、為欲隨說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科為欲隨說，為隨言說而有我語取。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6752"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲隨說分別所計作業受果所有士夫，及為隨說流轉還滅士夫之相，起我語取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我語取是執著種種我見之言語。為了想要隨言說分別計度所謂造作業力的人、受用果報的人以及流轉生死者、還歸寂滅者，便安立我在作業、我在受果，或我在流轉、我在證聖道；而有我的取著出現，因之生起我語取。若不明白業果只是諸行的流轉，便會取著有我、我所，以為有我在流轉、我在造業、我在修行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、取建立2　巳一、約二品辨4　午一、標為依</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科取建立，說明取的建立，分二科；第一科約二品辨，依二種品類分別，又分四科；第一科標為依，標示所依。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="63730:68384"></a>如是四取依於二品，謂受用欲諸在家品，及惡說法毗奈耶中諸出家品。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說的四取，是佛依於二種人來安立的，即：受用欲的在家人，以及惡說法與律的外道出家人。由這二類人容易生起的煩惱而安立四取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、簡此法3　未一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡此法，簡別此法，分三科；第一科標，標出要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由佛世尊每自稱言：我為諸取遍知、永斷正論大師。故於此法誓修行者，雖帶煩惱身壞命終，而不於彼建立諸取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於佛世尊常常自己說：「我普遍都知道種種取著的煩惱，我也永遠斷除煩惱現行及煩惱種子，我有正見相應的言論，這些教法是正確的，我是這樣的大師。」因此若有聽聞佛法、研究佛法，發願要修行者，雖然現在仍有煩惱未斷，命終時也還有煩惱，然而不依於佛弟子安立四種取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼佛弟子命終有煩惱，但不安立這四種取著？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於諸欲無所顧戀而出家故，於見、戒禁及以我語無執受故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　學習佛法的出家人需對色聲香味觸的諸欲沒有顧念愛惜才能捨家，因此不安立欲取。其次，由於聽聞佛法是與正見相應，沒有邪知邪見，故不安立見取。而佛所制的戒必定是與善法相應，因此也不會有外道錯誤的戒禁取，如持牛戒、狗戒等。且佛法主張無我，聖弟子若知道無我便不會說出有我。於未成就前，現在雖然有我，但是知道無我的道理，所以也不依佛弟子安立我語取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋建立2　未一、依惡說品2　申一、標列差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋建立，說明建立四取的原由，分二科；第一科依惡說品，依外道的惡說品類，分二科；第一科標列差別，標示列出差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">惡說法者有二差別。一、於見愛展轉發起怨諍論者，二、能證入世間定者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惡說法的外道出家人有二種差別。第一種人是思想上有愛著，愛著自宗的邪見，認為自宗的見是最殊勝的，展轉發起怨對乃至與正法產生諍論；第二種外道是還有修禪定者，可以證入世間定。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6753"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、配立二取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配立二取，配合所安立的二取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依於見愛展轉發起怨諍論者，建立見取；依能證入世間定者，立戒禁取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依於外道愛著錯誤的邪見，展轉發起怨恨諍論，建立見取；依外道之中能得世間禪定的人，建立戒禁取，因為這類人執著持某種戒才可以入定。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、依通二品</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依通二品，再依通於出家、在家人都會發生的煩惱，安立我語取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二品為依，執著我語，故依俱品立我語取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在家人與外道出家人，這二種人都會有我語取，外道出家人不知道無我的道理，在家人是指沒有學習佛法的人，也一定有我語取，由於這些人都不知道無我的道理，因此我語取是依二類人而安立。欲取則是特別依沒有學習佛法、顧戀諸欲的在家人而安立。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、釋名相3　未一、見</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋名相，解釋名相，分三科；第一科見，解釋見的名義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中見者，謂六十二，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四取中的見取，是指外道的六十二見，如前面已說應可了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂六十二如前應知者：前說：外道，薩迦耶見以為根本，有六十二諸惡見趣。謂四常見論、四一分常見論、二無因論、四有邊無邊想論、四不死矯亂論，如是十八諸惡見趣，是計前際說我論者。又有十六有想見論、八無想論、八非有想非無想論、七斷見論、五現法涅槃論，此四十四諸惡見趣，是計後際說我論者。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/87.htm#68400:66235">陵本八十七卷二頁6558</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道以我見為根本，而有六十二大類的諸惡見趣；包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四常見論、四一分常見論、二無因論、四有邊無邊想論、四不死矯亂論，這十八種邪見，是執著前一生有我而產生的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有十六有想見論、八無想論、八非有想非無想論、七斷見論、五現法涅槃論，這四十四種諸惡見趣，是執著來生有我而產生的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上總計六十二種諸惡見趣，如〈攝事分〉卷87，2584頁曾說過的，此處準照那裡應可了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、戒禁</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科戒禁，解釋戒禁的名義。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6754"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5365:68403"></a>邪分別見之所受持身護、語護，說名為戒；隨此所受形服、飲食、威儀行相，說名為禁。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處詳細的分別什麼是戒禁取的「戒」，由於有錯誤分別的思想，為了要保護身體不可作什麼，保護語言不可以說什麼，這都是戒；隨著執取錯誤的戒，而規定一定要穿什麼衣服、吃什麼食物，還有作些什麼特殊的威儀，則是戒禁取的「禁」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、我語2　申一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科我語，解釋我語的名義，分二科；第一科標，標出定義。</span></span></span></div>
