<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諦故、住故，論說有我，名為我語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諦，是真實。住，是執著。由於執著真的有我，而且住著有我，再以言論宣說有我，名為我語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">執有實物，說名諦故；執可安立，說名住故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　執著色受想行識內有一個真實的我住在其中，這真實的我名為諦；有一個名為諦的實物之後，又以名言安立它的名字，它的名字是「我」，執我是可用名言安立的，說名為住。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、約愛緣辨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約愛緣辨，約愛緣分別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於此中，欲愛為緣，建立欲取；依止智論，利養恭敬等愛為緣，建立見取；定愛為緣，立戒禁取；有無有愛為緣，立我語取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於其中，從愛緣分別，以欲愛為緣，對煩惱欲、事欲有愛著而建立欲取；依止有智慧的言論，愛著利養恭敬為緣而建立見取，外道也有似是而非的理論，所以依這些理論建立見取；為了得禪定，有很多錯誤的執取，如身護、語護，形服、飲食、威儀行相等，有很多禁止的事，依此安立戒禁取；有愛是通於三界的，屬於常見，無有愛則是斷見，執著我是常的或執著是斷，以這樣的愛著心為緣，安立我語取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十、四繫</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科繫，解釋四繫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當知四繫，唯依外道差別建立，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應知繫也有四種，這四種繫只依外道來建立，如前所說應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知四繫等者：謂貪身繫、瞋身繫、戒禁取身繫、此實執取身繫，是名四繫。唯依外道差別建立。能於色身、名身、趣向、所緣安住事中，令心繫縛，故名身繫。如前別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/87.htm#68412:66598">陵本八十七卷十四頁6593</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四繫分別是：貪身繫、瞋身繫、戒禁取身繫、此實執取身繫。這唯依外道而差別建立。由這四種繫，能令色身、名身、趣向、所緣等安住事中，令心被煩惱繫縛，故名身繫。如前面〈攝事分〉卷87，2598頁有各別解釋應該了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、貪身繫。貪是一種煩惱，指對欲的境界有種種的貪愛，一旦有這種繫縛的煩惱，將來會得到一個色受想行識蘊的五蘊身，這是由貪愛令有情結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、瞋身繫。即欲界的瞋恚，有瞋心的人不能脫離欲界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、戒禁取身繫。通於三界，除外道修習禪定之人有戒禁取，欲界的眾生也會有戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、此實執取身繫。又名我見身縛，由我見而增長諸惑業，束縛於身，名此實執取身繫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四種繫縛皆會使令有情在三界中得到下一生的果報。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6755"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十一、五蓋建立2　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五十一科五蓋建立，說明五蓋建立的原由，分二科；第一科標，標出要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，違背五處，當知建立五蓋差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，依違背五種處所，佛建立五種蓋的差別。蓋在前面的解釋是覆真實義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、列5　辰一、立貪欲蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種蓋，分五科；第一科立貪欲蓋，安立貪欲蓋的原由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、為在家諸欲境界所漂淪故，違背聖教，立貪欲蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、在家被色聲香味觸諸欲的境界所漂逆沈淪，違背聖教，因此安立貪欲蓋。雖在家人有欲的事，出家人沒有欲的事，然而若有欲的尋思，也是違背聖教。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、立瞋恚蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科立瞋恚蓋，安立瞋恚蓋的原由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、不堪忍諸同法者訶諫、驅擯、教誡等故，違背所有可愛樂法，立瞋恚蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由於不能堪忍共同修學佛法者的呵斥、勸諫、驅逐擯除、教授教誡等，違背所有可愛樂法（即六和敬），依此安立瞋恚蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、立惛沈睡眠蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科立惛沈睡眠蓋，安立惛沈睡眠蓋的原由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="8308:68421"></a>三、由違背奢摩他故，立惛沈睡眠蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、修定本應內心清醒的於所緣寂靜而住，但由於身心昏昧，或更進一步，闇昧到失去了所緣境，這都障礙定，因此安立惛沈睡眠蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、立掉舉惡作蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科立掉舉惡作蓋，安立掉舉惡作蓋的原由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、由違背毗鉢舍那故，立掉舉惡作蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、在修毗鉢舍那時本應正憶念，卻由於內心不寂靜，不能正憶念，違背了毗鉢舍那的緣故，而安立掉舉惡作蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、立疑蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科立疑蓋，安立疑蓋的原由。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、由違背於法論議無倒決擇、審察諸法大師聖教涅槃勝解故，建立疑蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由於對違背於正法的論議，不能沒有錯誤地決斷簡擇、審察諸法，對大師（佛）的聖教涅槃也沒有真實的勝解，因此建立疑蓋。尤其在佛法上對於法的論議，沒有得到正見便會有疑慮。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上說明五蓋安立的原由，〈決擇‧菩薩地〉卷77則將五蓋與所障法作分類：掉舉惡作，是奢摩他障；惛沈睡眠，是毘鉢舍那障；貪欲、瞋恚，當知俱障。其餘如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11與〈本地分‧聞所成地〉卷14等，也曾對五蓋作各別的解釋，可對應起來參考。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十二、株杌</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二株杌，解釋株杌的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6756"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若貪瞋癡纏所纏故，或彼隨眠所隨眠故，心不調柔，心極愚昧，於得自義能作衰損，故名株杌。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，株杌是良田中的障礙物。若有貪、瞋、癡的煩惱現行，或有貪瞋癡的種子在內心尚未斷除，心便不能調柔，十分剛強，內心這種極為愚癡昏昧的狀態，對於所要成就的涅槃功德會衰耗損壞，使令聖道不能成就，故名株杌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　株杌在前幾卷也曾說明過，如〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8云：「壞善稼田，故名株杌。」又如〈攝異門分〉卷84說：「又彼能令轉成上品相續起故，能令身心無堪能故；說為株杌。如舄鹵田，不任耕植」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十三、三垢3　卯一、貪垢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科三垢，解釋貪瞋癡三種污垢，分三科；第一科貪垢，說明貪垢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於弊下境所起貪欲，名為貪垢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，對三界粗弊低下之境所生起的貪欲，名為貪垢。如〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58說：「緣生受境（境界受）所起染著，說明為貪。」〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8 說：「自性染污，故名為垢。」意指煩惱以染污為自性，因此說名為垢。當有情對三有果報及三有的資具染著為性，能障無貪善根，生苦為業，名為貪垢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋垢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋垢，說明瞋垢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於不應瞋所緣境事所起瞋恚，名為瞋垢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於不應起瞋的所緣境事，心無慈悲，生起瞋恚；一旦有瞋，看什麼都不順心，總覺得別人與自己過不去，心非常的污穢，稱為瞋垢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　何謂不應瞋的所緣境事？於《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷44中說：「瞋有二種。一於應瞋處起，二於不應瞋處起。前名為恚，後名為害。彼二相應尋名恚尋害尋，故有差別。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　害謂瞋之一分，以無哀無悲無愍為體，損惱有情為業。如《成唯識論》卷6說：「云何為害？於諸有情，心無悲愍；損惱為性。能障不害，逼惱為業。謂有害者，逼惱他故，此亦瞋恚一分為體，離瞋無別害相用故。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝異門分〉卷84也說：「又害者，謂顯示攝受上品怨嫌故。」因此一旦有害，便會逼惱有情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡垢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡垢，說明癡垢的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於極顯現、愚癡眾生尚能了事所起愚癡，名為癡垢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於極為明顯的、愚癡眾生尚且都能了知的事，卻於內心生起愚癡，名為癡垢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十四、燒害</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科燒害，說明燒害的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若貪瞋癡數數現行，恆常流溢，燒惱身心，極為衰損，說名燒害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若貪瞋癡的煩惱常常現行，煩惱常從六根流漏出來，燒惱自己的身心，使身心受到很大的衰敗損害，這樣的煩惱名為燒害。另外，燒害也形容煩惱的過患。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8中曾說到燒害，但將二字分開解釋：「能令所欲，常有匱乏，故名為燒。」又說：「常能為害故，名為常害。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十五、箭</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科箭，說明煩惱為也名為箭。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若貪瞋癡遠離慚愧，無慚愧故，一向無間，不可制伏，定為傷損，說名為箭。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果因貪瞋癡的煩惱而遠離慚愧，由於無慚無愧的緣故，能令有情一直無間的生長惡行、毀犯戒律，因此煩惱如射箭一般，一旦射出，便不會停止，毒箭一直向前，無法控制，最終必定傷害損惱有情，所以煩惱也名為箭。另外，凡夫由於煩惱入胎，故也以箭來形容，如〈本地分‧意地〉卷2 說：若已結凝，「箭」內仍稀，名羯羅藍。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8則說箭是不靜相故，遠所隨故。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6757"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十六、所有</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科所有，煩惱也名所有，這是指煩惱能攝受五蘊的果報體，主導有情的身語意去造業，由愛取有，而取得五蘊。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若貪瞋癡慚愧間雜，由相續故非剎那故，有可制伏，說名所有，是繫所攝極下穢義。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若有貪瞋癡的煩惱，又有無慚無愧間雜在其中，由於煩惱是相續的，因此有力讓心被煩惱所制伏，說名所有，是貪等四種身繫所攝，有非常卑下污穢之義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是繫所攝極下穢義者：前說：貪欲身繫攝貪所有，瞋恚身繫攝瞋所有，餘二身繫攝癡所有。當知此中，極鄙穢義是所有義。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/87.htm#68442:66963">陵本八十七卷二十四頁6626</a>）此應準釋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪欲身繫是屬於貪所有，瞋恚身繫是屬於瞋所有，戒禁取身繫及此實執取餘二身繫，是癡所有。當知煩惱極為鄙下污穢，即是所有義。在〈攝事分〉卷87，2609頁曾說明過，此處應準照那裏解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第228頁：入處相應第58經；累計經數236經；大正藏（201）經<br />
　如是我聞：一時，佛住舍衛國祇樹給孤獨園。時有異比丘來詣佛所，稽首佛足，退坐一面。白佛言：「世尊！云何知、云何見，次第疾得漏盡」？爾時、世尊告彼比丘：「當正觀無常。何等法無常？謂眼無常，若色、眼識、眼觸、眼觸因緣生受── 若苦、若樂、不苦不樂，當觀無常。耳&hellip;&hellip;。鼻&hellip;&hellip;。舌&hellip;&hellip;。身&hellip;&hellip;。意當觀無常，若法、意識、意觸、意觸因緣生受──若苦、若樂、不苦不樂，彼亦無常。比丘！如是知、如是見，次第盡有漏」。時彼比丘聞佛所說，歡喜作禮而去。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛在舍衛國祇樹給孤獨園，有另外一位比丘來拜訪佛，請問佛說：「您的智慧如何見到過去、現在、未來這些境界，又如何觀察境界，才能令煩惱能夠很快的斷盡？」這時，佛開示他無常觀，應觀察六根、六塵、六識、六觸、六受都是無常的，時常這樣觀察便能次第的斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第228頁：入處相應第59〜74經；累計經數237〜252經；大正藏（ ）經<br />
　如是比丘所說經，若差別者：云何知、云何見，次第盡一切結，斷一切縛，斷一切使，斷一切上煩惱，斷一切結，斷諸流，斷諸軛，斷諸取，斷諸觸，斷諸蓋，斷諸纏，斷諸垢，斷諸愛，斷諸意，斷邪見生正見，斷無明生明。「比丘！如是觀眼無常，乃至如是知、如是見，次第無明斷明生」。時彼比丘聞佛所說歡喜，歡喜已作禮而去。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第59到74經都與58經相同，只是觀察所要斷除的煩惱不同，因此本論中廣說煩惱，用以解釋59到74經所說的眾多煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　像比丘所說經一樣（指58經），差別只在於，將「次第疾得漏盡」，換成「次第盡一切結」，結是三結；或換成「斷一切縛」，即三縛；以及「斷一切使」，十使；「斷一切上煩惱」，所有的煩惱。論中又解釋隨煩惱，所有的煩惱都是隨煩惱，四十八種加五種，共說了五十三種；「斷一切結」，包括九結；「斷諸流」是四暴流；「斷諸軛」，是四軛；「斷諸取」，四取；「斷諸觸」，無明相應觸；「斷諸蓋」，五蓋。「斷諸纏」，八纏；「斷諸垢」，三垢；「斷諸愛」的三愛；「斷諸意」，依論文是斷燒、有見、所有這三法；乃至「斷邪見生正見」，「斷無明生明」。這樣共有十六部經。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是第一個別頌中，煩惱的部分，接著論中再說明業，業的雜染可配合〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9、〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59、與卷60。本卷89則是配合經文來詳細說明業雜染，以及業的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑八、廣說業2　寅一、業雜染2　卯一、唯惡行攝2　辰一、釋體義3　巳一、出體2　午一、舉不善身業</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科廣說業，此為「處擇攝」第一個總頌的第一個別頌（安立攝）中，第三句「解脫煩惱業」的「業」，詳細說明業，分二科；第一科業雜染，說明業雜染，雜染是與染相雜，由於造業時與煩惱在一起，故名業雜染，又分二科，第一科唯惡行攝，唯是惡行所攝，又分二科；第一科釋體義，解釋惡業的體性、名詞及義理，又分三科；第一科出體，說出不善業的體性，又分二科；第一科舉不善身業，舉不善身業為例。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業的自性是造作，由內心的意相應思先造作，之後的身行、語行才顯現。心中先有造作是思業，有了行動是思已業，這是業的自性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，一切不善身業名為惡行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，一切不善的身業，包括殺盗婬，都是屬於不善的身業，都名為惡行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例語意二業</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例語意二業，例說語、意二種惡業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如說身業，語業、意業，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說的身惡業，不善的語業是妄言、綺語、惡口、兩舌；意業是指貪、瞋、癡，這些也都屬於惡行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋名</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋名，解釋名詞，約果報來形容惡行，時常造這種業能種下三惡道的種子，招感三惡道果報，因此名為惡行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此惡業數現行故，於諸惡趣或已隨得、或當隨得、或現隨得，是故說彼名為惡行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這類身口意惡業數數現行的緣故，於三惡趣，或已得惡趣種子的隨逐、或者將來會得到惡趣的果報、甚至或現在惡業種子已成熟使令果報正得。以上無論是在種子狀態，或約將來、或約現在得果而言，都說這種不善的身語意業名為惡行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　但是，如果惡業已被懺悔則不增長，不一定會到三惡道去。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6758"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或已隨得等者：隨謂隨逐，麤重所攝。得謂證得，彼果所攝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨是隨逐，指過去造作的惡業，已種下種子，而惡業的種子比較麤重，能令行者沒有堪能性。如〈本地分‧意地〉卷2所說：「又於諸自體中所有種子、若煩惱品所攝；名為粗重，亦名隨眠。若異熟品所攝、及餘無記品所攝；唯名粗重，不名隨眠。若信等善法品所攝種子，不名粗重，亦非隨眠。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得是指將來會得果報；造這種惡業會得到三惡道的果報，或當隨得，未來惡業的種子才會待緣成熟，或現隨得，現在便有果報。這是約時間來分別惡行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、顯義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯義，顯示不善業的道理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此示現業雜染義。煩惱雜染前已顯了。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此開示顯發出業雜染的道理。而煩惱雜染前文已詳細的說明了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、辨安立2　巳一、標列二論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨安立，辨別邪正二論的安立，分二科；第一科標列二論，標示列舉出二種對業的看法，一種正確，一種不正確。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，有二安立業雜染論。一者、邪論，二者、正論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，又有二種以語言文字來安立的業雜染。一、邪論，即外道的論點。二、正論，依正見而安立的言論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別釋其相2　午一、邪論3　未一、舉論說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋其相，各別解釋正邪二論的相貌，分二科；第一科邪論，說明邪論，又分三科；第一科舉論說，舉出外道邪論的說法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">言邪論者，謂如是說：若有故思，凡所造作諸不善業，一切決定當受惡趣。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所謂邪論方面，是指如果有人這樣說：「若有故意造作諸不善業，一定會到三惡道去受果報。」佛弟子應該知道，這樣說會有過失，是不對的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、斥彼非3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科斥彼非，破斥外道的錯誤，分三科；第一科標，標出過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此論便謗修行梵行能證涅槃。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這種外道的言論會毀謗修行梵行能證涅槃的聖道，令人不能修道證果。這是將業果的道理說死了，決定如此，其實不決定。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼是錯的？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6759"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸有情類不易可得，於現法中無有故思造不善業，況在餘生。若彼決定感惡趣者，便應無有解脫可得。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所有的有情在今生當中，不容易都沒有作過任何故思造的不善業，何況在餘生。凡夫有情的起心動念由於有俱生我法二執，故無不是業，無不是罪，很難完全沒有故思所造的不善業，這樣的心念太多了，今生是這樣，過去或未來也一樣。而外道的理論是造了故思不善業，一定會到三惡道去受果，那麼就沒有解脫的可能了，因此這樣說是不正確的邪論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結當知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結當知，結說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故當知此為邪論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此應當知道這樣具有自性執的業果道理是錯誤的邪論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、正論2　未一、舉論說2　申一、亦作亦增長業</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科正論，說明正論的體相，分二科；第一科舉論說，舉出正論所說，又分二科；第一科亦作亦增長業，造作也增長的惡業才會招感惡趣果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若如是說：諸有故思造不善業，此業亦作亦增長者，定於當來受不可愛惡趣異熟。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有人這樣說：凡是經過審慮思惟後造的不善業，作了以後還不斷增長，將來一定會招感不可愛三惡道的果報。〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60說什麼是增長；若於所作數隨尋伺，每尋伺一次就增長業的力量，名增長業。〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58說具三因緣能往惡趣：1、於欲界煩惱極多修習，殷重、無間計為功德，不見其失、不見其患，縱情而起。2、用此煩惱以為依處，由身語意，於諸惡行作及增長。3、由此煩惱斷他善品，授不善品。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、雖作不增長業2　酉一、明順受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科雖作不增長業，雖然有造作但是業不增長，分二科；第一科明順受，說明有順苦樂受。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有雖作不增長者，彼彼法受為依止故，諸所造作或樂、或苦，當於造時，於現法中，此業決定或順樂受、或順苦受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然造作了業，業不增長，但還是會得果報的，法受，作善法或不善法所生的感受，包括今生及來生，有四種法受：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、今生受樂，來生受苦異熟果：指與喜樂俱造十惡業。例如今生造十惡業時很高興，苦果是來生會到三惡道去。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、今生受苦，來生受樂：這是與憂苦俱修十善。例如今生被教導要修十善業，不殺生、不偷盜、不邪淫時，感覺蠻苦惱的，很勉強的修十善業，可是來生感得的是人天的善果，快樂的異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、今生受樂，來生也受樂：這是與喜樂俱修十善業。例如今生修善法時心裡是很歡喜快樂的，來生的果報也是很歡喜快樂的；或與喜樂俱修其它的正行也是一樣，今生受樂，來生也受樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、今生受苦，來生也受苦：這是與憂苦俱造十惡業。例如今生造十惡業時是憂愁苦惱的，來生也是到三惡道去受苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造善業時不論是與樂受或苦受，將來一定是得到樂果，這是順樂受。如果造的是惡業，不論現在是痛苦或是快樂，將來會得到苦受，這是順苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《中阿含經》中的《受法經》，舉例子說明法受與果報的關係，比如這人造了不善業，雖然現在很快樂，因為造的是不善業，將來會得到苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如沙門婆羅門有欲，為求快樂的享受欲樂，而造作不善法，將來會得到苦果，這是順苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造不善業與苦受在一起是煩惱的，將來也一樣受苦果，指裸形外道，如前所說的戒禁取，用手或樹葉當他的衣服，不可用水瓶來喝水，只可以用手捧來喝等，這樣的苦行都是有煩惱的不善業，且與苦受俱行，將來還是苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種善法受，現在雖受苦，將來會得到順樂受的果報；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果一類人有很嚴重的貪瞋癡，非常的苦惱，還是來佛法裡面修行，要這類人離貪瞋癡是很苦惱的，不過此類人還能勉強自己，盡這一生修行梵行，乃至離欲，因此命終之後終會到善處。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種修離欲行，能離貪瞋癡，不但現在很快樂，將來也會得到快樂的果報，這種人煩惱很薄，修行是很快樂的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造業時的感受不能影響將來所得的果報是苦或是樂，而是由所造業的性質是善業或不善業來決定將來的善惡果報。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6760"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼彼法受為依止故等者：此中義顯順所受業。或順樂受、或順苦受，然以法受為依，或樂、或苦，而非一向由樂俱行、或苦俱行。業各有順樂、順苦差別，不決定故。集論中說：樂俱行業，順樂受者，還受樂異熟；順苦受者，還受苦異熟；順不苦不樂受者，還受不苦不樂異熟。苦俱行業，順樂受者，還受樂異熟；順苦受者，還受苦異熟；順不苦不樂受者，還受不苦不樂異熟。（集論五卷七頁）由是此說，諸所造作或樂、或苦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡的義理是顯示造業後將來會得到什麼樣的果報。順所受業，有二種；一種是順樂受，將來受人天快樂的果報；另一種是順苦受，到三惡道去受苦報，人天受報是苦樂夾雜，有時快樂有時痛苦。以法受為依，法是指善法或不善法，是約業的性質來決定將來的果報。而不是以造業時與樂受在一起的樂俱行，或苦受在一起的苦俱行，決定將來是順樂受或順苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》中說：與樂受在一起造業是樂俱行業，造業時候很快樂有三種情況；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、若造業時很快樂，業的性質是屬於善業是順樂受，順樂受者將來必定得到快樂的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、現在很安樂，是富貴之人，可是造作殺盗婬妄不善業，是順苦受。雖然造業時很快樂，由於業的性質是屬於不善的，將來會受到苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、不苦不樂受有二種，一種是有煩惱而造業，一種是與善心所在一起造善業，又有一種是無記業，是順不苦不樂受者。將來得到的是不苦不樂的異熟。譬如種種的工巧業處，是不苦不樂相應的，將來的等流習氣，即對某一方面有專長，隨順領受不苦不樂異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦俱行業也與樂俱行業一樣，造業時痛苦的感覺也有三種情況：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、順樂受者，還受樂異熟，欲、煩惱很重的人來修行，雖然修得很勉強、很憂愁，不過所造業的性質是善的，屬於順樂受的業，將來會得到人天的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、順苦受者，還受苦異熟。邪見的外道修苦行，如一日只吃幾口飯，或持牛戒、狗戒，現在很苦將來也會得到苦的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、順不苦不樂受者，還受不苦不樂異熟。現在很苦，造的業是屬於無記業，無記業得的是不苦不樂捨受相應，將來也會受不苦不樂受的異熟。這是在《集論》卷5，7頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、辨追悔2　戌一、無追悔</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨追悔，辨別追悔的相貌，分二科；第一科無追悔，無有追悔情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸有造作如是業已，若無追悔、不修對治補特伽羅，彼於此業若更增長、若不增長，此業雖定順現法受，亦轉令成順惡趣受，於現法中能障解脫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有人造作惡業以後，內心對所造惡業從不回顧後悔，又沒有修止觀來對治惡法，對於故思所造的惡業，不斷的尋思令業增長，或不相續業沒有再增長，這種內心完全不悔過的情況，是為增長業，這一生一定會得到苦果，這是順現法得到苦受，來生也會轉變成順生受的惡趣。在現在的生命體當中能障礙解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、有追悔</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有追悔，說明有追悔的情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸有造作如是業已，若生追悔、修習對治補特伽羅，彼於此業若不增長、若更增長，此業雖是順惡趣受，亦轉令成順現法受，不障解脫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造作惡業以後，若是追悔了，或是修奢摩他毗鉢舍那對治煩惱，這樣的有情，於故思所造業，不論它增不增長，都有對治，又不斷懺悔，是為不增長業，其所造的業雖然當來要到三惡道去受，由於懺悔、對治，也會轉成今生重罪輕報的順現法受，不會障礙解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結當知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結當知，結說應當知道的正論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故此論，不名誹謗修習梵行能證涅槃。當知此論是為正論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是這樣的主張，不名為誹謗修習梵行能證涅槃，應當知道這樣的言論才是正確的言論。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然造了惡業但已追悔、有對治，這種業不論有沒有增長，它不障礙解脫，而且這順生受的惡趣果，也轉成順現受。如果沒有追悔又不對治，其故思所造業，雖然是順現法受，也會轉變成來生順生受的惡趣，在現法中會障礙解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6761"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此業雖定順現法受等者：順生現苦，名順現法受。順生當苦，名順惡趣受。此中義顯業有轉變，應受現法輕苦，轉成當來惡趣重苦故。下說追悔、修習對治補特伽羅，與此相違，應知其相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順生現法苦，名順現法受。順生當來苦受，名順惡趣受。這其中的道理顯示業有轉變，本來應受現法輕苦的，因為無追悔、不修對治，轉成未來到三惡道受重苦的果報。反之，下面說追悔、修習對治的人，則與此相反，即將順惡趣受轉成今生重罪輕報的順現法受，不障礙現法解脫，應該知道其中相狀。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、通諸業攝3　辰一、明對治3　巳一、標具闕</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科通諸業攝，通於各種業所攝的對治、安住與施設，分三科；第一科明對治，說明由惡業的有無對治而成染淨，又分三科；第一科標具闕，標出具足對治成淨或闕少對治成染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有闕於十種對治，為業雜染之所染汙；若有會遇如是十種，便得清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果於故思惡業闕乏十種對治，便被業雜染所染污；如果有這十種對治，便可得到清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列種類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列種類，列出十種對治。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、若由如是對治，雖有作業，而無增長，彼望當來成不定受。二者、若由如是對治，雖未永斷而更不受。三者、若由如是對治，永斷離繫。四者、守護諸根門故，善修其身，為欲修習增上戒學。五者、修習增上戒已，為欲修習增上心學。六者、修習增上心已，為欲修習增上慧學。七者、修習增上慧已，為斷諸漏。八者、猛利意樂修習。九者、長時修習。十者、無量門對治修習。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、如果有這十種對治，惡業雖然已經造了，由於修習對治，此業作而不增長，來生是不定受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、如果有這十種對治，雖然沒有永遠斷除業種子，可是不會再受果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、如果透過這樣對治的方法，能永遠斷除煩惱種子，離開三界的繫縛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、守護六根，修根律儀，善巧的修治自己的身語意，是以修習增上戒學，來對治惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、修習增上戒已，是為了修習增上定學，以定來降伏煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、修習增上心學已，是為了修習增上慧學，以慧來對治煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、修習增上慧學已，是為了斷除各種煩惱種子，證得解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、在修習戒定慧，或在懺悔時，具有很猛利的修習意樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、長時間的懺悔及修習戒定慧三學。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、用無量門來修習對治修習，如懺悔，修戒定慧、根律儀，或其它善法，以此種種對治法使令業障消除。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、結染淨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結染淨，結說業的染淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有不會如是十種業對治者，為業雜染之所染汙；與此相違，當知清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果不努力修這十種業的對治，會被業雜染所染污。業雜染包括行善業也可能是雜染，因為行善中沒有佛法無漏的智慧，所修的善都與我執相應而不清淨，還會到人天受報。所以必須要修戒定慧，而且要猛利修習，長時修習，以無量門對治修習等，應當了知此十種對治能令心清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6762"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、辨安住3　巳一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨安住，辨別安住於對治道中的相狀，分三科；第一科總標，總相標出要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於現法中，不善防護身語意業而住者，彼先造作惡不善業亦令增長，於當來世令其雜染。若善防護身語意業而住者，彼不雜染。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在現在的生命體當中，如果不能善巧防護身語意業而安住的人，也會使令過去所造作惡不善業增長，於來生有業雜染及生雜染。如果現在能夠精勤的防護身語意業而安住的人，能夠修戒律儀、根律儀、戒定慧，則不雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、雙徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科雙徵，雙問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何於現法中，不善防護身語意業而住？云何善防護身語意業而住？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是在現在的生命體當中，不善防護身語意業而住？什麼情況又是善防護身語意業而住？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、別釋2　午一、不善防護2　未一、出種類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別釋，各別解釋，分二科；第一科不善防護，說明不善防護的情形，分二科；第一科出種類，說出種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不善防護身語意業而住者，謂如有一，於諸不善身語意業纏所發起，能誓遠離；然於能起不正作意相應無明，猶故發起。又於諸善身語意業受學隨轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不善防護身語意業而住的人，是指有一類人，對於不善的身語意業是煩惱所發動的，雖然能發誓遠離，但不知道造業的原因是有不如理作意相應的我執無明所引，由於無明還在，由不如理作意發起不善的身語意業。雖然依佛教法或依師長的教誨，修習善的身語意業，由此善的福業及不動業仍會招感後有的果報，依後有果報為依還會生起雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又於諸善身語意業受學隨轉者：福、不動行，總名諸善身語意業。彼於因果不知出離，唯依教法，或依誨法，亦於能起不正作意相應無明，猶故發起，是名受學隨轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　福行、不動行，總名為諸善的身語意業。這類人對於出離三界的因果不明，不如實知道諦與滅諦的修證，唯依佛的教法或依師長的教誨法，也能起不正作意相應的我執無明，還會發起後有的福業及非福業，是名受學隨轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此因緣，於現法中，於諸煩惱、邪欲尋求、所作眾苦無有差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這樣的因緣，看不清楚什麼是無明，不知道最根本的問題在有我執與法執，雖然修習福業及不動業，因為煩惱引起的邪欲尋求，將來得到生雜染眾苦是沒有差別的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、明雜染</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明雜染，說明雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6763"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼唯即於此誓受遠離，便生喜足，於現法中不起聖道，不證涅槃。彼雖如是防護而住，於現法中暫時不作惡不善業，然為煩惱隨眠纏縛。既終歿已，後有續生；隨所受身，依先業緣廣起雜染。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類人只是於此不善業發願遠離，願意受戒遠離不善業，覺得自己這樣持戒就夠了，而生滿足，在現法中不修止不修觀，不證聖道，不成就涅槃的功德。雖然也是修很多防護而住，在現在的生命體當中，因為有決定要持戒，暫時不會作惡不善業，然而還有煩惱現行，被煩惱種子所纏縛。這是不正作意相應我執無明猶在，這類人死後還會再有下一個生命體，隨業力所得到的果報身會有等流性，由過去造業的因緣還會生起煩惱、業、生等種種雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於諸煩惱邪欲尋求所作眾苦者：謂生等苦，隨業所作，業復以諸煩惱邪欲尋求為其因緣。此中義顯煩惱、業、生三種雜染，如次配釋應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生老病死憂悲苦惱等生雜染，是隨順業力所生起，業又是依種種煩惱起邪欲尋求為其因緣而生起。這其中的義理顯示煩惱、業、生三種雜染，如它的次第配合解釋應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、善防護2　未一、標列差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科善防護，說明善防護的體相，分二科；第一科標列差別，標示列出與不善防護的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若善防護身語意業而住者，有此差別。謂此依彼誓受遠離，不造新業，故業雖熟，暫觸異熟尋能變吐。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善防護身語意業而住的行者，有這種差別。指依止先前受戒時所發遠離惡法的誓願，不再造新業，因此即使舊業成熟現在眼前，有誓願力故，才剛剛碰觸到果報緣境，馬上即能將它斷除，轉染成淨不令相續。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、成善護住2　申一、由無雜染3　酉一、標堪能</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成善護住，成就善護安住，分二科；第一科，由無雜染，由無有雜染方面說明成就善護安住的功德，又分三科；第一科標堪能，標出能有堪能性成就聖道證得涅槃。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼唯於此誓受遠離不生喜足，於現法中能起聖道，亦能證得彼果涅槃。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類人對於唯有誓受遠離雜染而持戒清淨的功德並不生歡喜滿足，不會認為持戒清淨就夠了，深知持戒清淨雖可感人天善報，仍然還在生死雜染中，因此進一步修定修慧，在現在的生命體當中能生起聖道，成就無分別智，證得涅槃的功德。這是因為成就善護安住而能有堪能性成就聖道、證得涅槃。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋證得2　戌一、有餘依涅槃</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋證得，解釋善護安住所證得的果位，分二科；第一科有餘依涅槃，說明有餘依涅槃的境界。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於爾時，乃至有識身相續住，恆受先業所感諸受。於現法中，彼有識身，乃至壽量未滅盡位，常相續住。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已成就善護安住證得涅槃的行者，其時果報體還在，還是恆常領受過去業力所感諸苦受、樂受、不苦不樂受。在現在的生命體當中，這有識身是先業所感得的果報，在壽量未滅盡以前還是相續而住，過去的業不斷的觸到異熟，果報會現前，但不會再起煩惱造業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6764"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、無餘依涅槃</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無餘依涅槃，說明無餘依涅槃的境界。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壽量若盡，捨有識身，於後命根更不成就。由是因緣，識與一切諸受俱滅，後不相續，彼如影受與其識樹皆滅盡故，遍於一切不可施設。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿羅漢壽量若盡，捨離有識身後，便無後有命根的因緣。由於壽命盡的因緣，入無餘依涅槃後，阿羅漢的心識與所有一切諸受果報，都同時不可得，不再相續。此生是最後一生的果報，不會再有下一生，這些受像是樹的影子，樹譬如他的心識，「彼如影受與其識樹皆滅盡故」這一句話表示萬法唯心所造。眾生的諸受是由心造業而感得的，心識像一棵樹，心造了業會有果報，好像太陽照下去會有影子。如果入無餘依涅槃，心不可得，果報也不可得，不能施設說此人到三界五趣哪裡去，因為根本不可得，在三界五趣中不再有命根，所以遍一切處不可施設。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、攝略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科攝略義，要略歸納要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於爾時，由二因緣，先所作業於當來世不能為染。一、由煩惱為其助伴令雜染者無餘斷故；二、由依此諸行相續成熟雜染無餘滅故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者證得阿羅漢時，由二種因緣，過去生所造業力於未來世不能再有染污的力量。一、成就盡智，一切作為生雜染助伴緣的愛見煩惱全都無餘永斷。二、得到無生智，由於所依的愛見煩惱永斷故，使令色受想行識無法相續成熟，未來的生雜染也都全部斷滅了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、由證恆住2　酉一、釋多差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由證恆住，由證恆住方面說明成就善護安住的功德，阿羅漢有六恆住，當六根接觸六塵時，一切時住最上捨，不會再起愛見煩惱，分二科；第一科釋多差別，解釋有多種差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於爾時，諸有情所善友意樂相續轉故，名無怨心；於彼所緣瞋恚斷故，名無恚心；於業異熟深見過患增上緣力誓遠離故，名無染心；已具獲得能對治彼諸聖道故，名無顛倒善解脫心。彼由如是，能具證得六種恆住。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者成就阿羅漢果時，於諸有情所是善友意樂相續而轉，名無怨心。對所有緣境由於瞋恚已斷，不會有任何不高興，名無恚心。由於深見業果異熟過患的增上緣力故，發誓遠離流轉，不再來生死中受苦，名無染心。已具足獲得能對治諸雜染的聖道，通達無常苦空無我的真理，善巧解脫愛見煩惱，名無顛倒善解脫心。行者由於如是具足上述無怨心、無恚心、無染心、無顛倒善解脫心，能永斷煩惱，成就阿羅漢果，具足證得六種恆住。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、結異先住</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結異先住，結說善防護住與先前所說不善防護住的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有於彼多所住者，於現法中，雖有種種諸惡不善業緣間雜，由此遠離，一向成善。由是因緣，當知此與先防護住有其差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有善防護身語意業而住多修習的行者，證得阿羅漢有無顛倒的善解脫心，才能夠多所住。在現在的生命體當中，阿羅漢已經成就心遠離，所行一向成善法，所以雖然也因過去所造惡業而有種種不善的業緣間雜顯現，也能身苦心不苦。由於這樣的因緣，應當知道善防護身語意業而住與之前所說不善防護住是有差別的。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6765"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若有於彼多所住者等者：謂如前說，於善防護身語意業而住多修習故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所說，善防護是包括修戒定慧、誓受遠離、不造新業、能起聖道、能修涅槃，這樣是真正究竟的善防護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、辨施設3　巳一、施設領受業異熟論2　午一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨施設，辨明種種業行施設，分三科；第一科施設領受業異熟論，說明施設造業得異熟果的言論，又分二科；第一科總標，總相標出各由五相成染淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當知施設領受業異熟論，由五種相成其雜染，由五種相成不雜染。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當知道所有以名言施設造業感得異熟果的言論，由五種相貌知其為染污邪論，又由五種相知其為清淨正論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、別辨2　未一、成雜染3　申一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別分辨邪論與正論，分二科；第一科成雜染，說明成雜染的邪論，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為由五種相成其雜染？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是由五種相使令言論成為雜染的？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由施設惡因論故，亦由施設無因論故，及由施設惡因、無因有三過故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一相，施設惡因論，主張生命是由大梵天等創造，所說生命現起的原因是錯誤的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二相，施設無因論，主張有情世間生起的原因是無因而有的，這也是邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三相，即施設惡因、無因的第一種過失，以為現在一切苦受全是由宿業或由現在為因的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四相，即施設惡因、無因的第二種過失，毀謗精進的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五相，即施設惡因、無因的第三種過失，毀謗正智的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋3　酉一、施設惡因論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科施設惡因論，說明施設惡因論的內容。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中施設惡因論者，謂如有一，起如是見，立如是論：若有士夫補特伽羅，諸所領受，一切皆是宿因所作。如是或謂自在、變化等因所作。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中施設錯誤的因果論方面，如有一類人生起這樣的見地，安立這樣的言論：有情現在所領受的一切果報，全都是過去宿因所作。或者認為世間萬物，必定另外有一個主宰者，稱為作者；另外有一個可以出生這些事情的生者；以及另外有能變化世間萬物的主人，如大自在天；或者是其他的大梵天王等，總之一定有一個主宰者在操縱。惡因論有這二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在受果報的原因不一定全部都是過去生所造的，也有現在造的，如果全部都是宿因所作，則現在的努力便無意義，因為一切都注定了，與因緣生法相違，所以是有過失的。或是說現在的果報，都是由大自在天或是上帝決定的，他作自受，也不正確。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、施設無因論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科施設無因論，解釋施設無因論的內容。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">施設無因論者，謂如有一，起如是見，立如是論：若有士夫補特伽羅，諸所領受，當知一切無因無緣。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　施設無因論方面，是有一類外道生起這樣的思想，安立這樣的言論：所有有情現在所領受的一切果報，應當知道都是沒有因緣而有的，這是無因論。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6766"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、施設惡因無因有三種過2　戌一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科施設惡因無因有三種過，說明施設惡因無因有三種過失，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何施設惡因、無因有三種過？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說施設錯誤的惡因及無因論有三種過失？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋2　亥一、別辨相3　天一、諸不善受因不成過3　地一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別辨明其中的相貌，又分三科；第一科諸不善受因不成過，說明主張諸不善受是由過去或現在不善業為因的過失，又分三科；第一科標，標出過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂現法中，不善俱行不善諸受，宿世業為因亦有過失，現法業為因亦有過失。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若認為在現在生命體當中，與不善業俱行的不善諸受，包括樂、苦二受，如與憂苦俱造十惡業（不善的苦受），或與喜樂俱造十惡業（不善的樂受），全都是以宿世業為因，這是有過失的。若說不是過去的宿因，全都是由現在造業為因，也還是有過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋2　玄一、宿業為因2　黃一、標過</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科宿業為因，說明主張所有諸受全以宿業為因的過失，又分二科；第一科標過，標出其中的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若言此受宿世惡業以為因者，是則有一，依於不善諸樂法受，而有其樂不善受生，此用宿世諸不善業以為因生，不應道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有人主張現在的不善苦樂二受（即上文所說與不善業俱行的苦樂二受）全是由於過去的惡業為因，是則認為有情現在與喜樂俱行的不善業受生（現在造不善業很歡喜快樂），都是依於過去不善業諸樂法受（過去生很歡喜快樂造不善業）而來。假如用宿世諸不善業以為因而生出今生快樂的果報，這是不合道理的。因為得人身是快樂的果報，這快樂的果報並非以宿世諸不善業為因而生出的，現在說依此果報與喜樂俱行造不善業（以歡喜快樂的心情造惡業），是由於過去造不善業與樂受相應而感得，這是以邪論推託現在生歡喜造惡業的理由全都是因為過去生也是以喜樂心造不善業，這是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依於不善諸樂法受等者：謂依過去不善諸樂法受，應感苦異熟果。而於現法感樂異熟不善受生，謂是宿業為因，不應道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去所造的不善業，雖然與諸快樂的法受在一起，仍應感得苦的異熟果。而於現法感得樂異熟不善受生，說是以宿業為因，是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　果報的受苦受樂是由過去業的性質來決定的；如果過去造的是不善業，雖然造業時與樂受在一起，也應該是感得苦的異熟果，不應感得樂不善受。若認為現在的快樂果報是由於過去所造不善業所感得，以過去不善諸樂法受為因，就不合道理了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、釋非</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋非，解釋它的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？非彼宿世諸不善業於現法中感樂異熟，應正道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？並不是過去造不善業，在現法中會感得樂受的異熟果，這樣說才是相應於正確的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若說在現法中可以感得快樂的異熟，是由於過去的不善業為因，這是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、現業為因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科現業為因，說明主張所有諸受全以現業為因的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6767"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若言此受用現法中惡業為因，是則退失自意所立諸惡因論及無因論，謂諸所受皆宿因作，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是舉例，如果主張現在所受用的一切苦果都是以現在造惡業為因的話，則與自己所安立的諸惡因論或無因論相矛盾。宿因論即惡因論，是主張所有異熟全都是由於過去的宿因而來，或自在天變化所作，乃至廣說或是無因論所主張的無因而有，這二種過失，如前已說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名初過。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是名第一種過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》乃至廣說者：謂如前說，自在變化等因所作，或復一切無因無緣，是名廣說應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所說，外道邪論主張現在造的業或受的果都是以過去宿世業為因，或是自在天等，有能夠變化世間萬物的主人變化所作，或一切是無因無緣而有，是名廣說，應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、謗精進過</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科謗精進過，說明施設惡因、無因論會有第二種毀謗精進的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又若說言：諸不善法皆用宿世惡業為因。是則決定所有善法，亦用宿世善法為因。如是所有不善對治，諸善加行俱生精進，皆成無用。如是名為第二過失。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若如前說，所有不善法都是以宿世的惡業為因，是則決定主張所有善法也是以宿世的善法為因，如此將所有的業果，善不善法都歸諸於過去生決定，則現在所有對治不善業而精進加行的善業，也都成為毫無作用了。如是名為第二種過失，毀謗精進的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、謗正智過2　地一、辨2　玄一、舉難2　黃一、無觀察智難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科謗正智過，說明施設惡因、無因論會有第三種毀謗聖人智慧的過失，分二科；第一科辨，分別，又分二科；第一科舉難，舉出難問，又分二科；第一科無觀察智難，對於不需觀察智的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又若現在無有士用，是則應無依善不善審正觀察是所應作、所不應作。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次如果主張一切都是以過去所造業為因，或大自在天等為因，或無因論，則現法的努力都沒有作用了，應該也無依止善法或不善法的不同，所以也不需要仔細正確的觀察善是應該作的、不善是不應該作的，不用修行了。因為所有的事都被過去生決定了，或無因而有，這些正確的智慧觀察也都徒勞無功了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、無如實智難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無如實智難，沒有如實智的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又如實智應成無用。謂了知已，此我應轉、此我應成。</span></strong></span></span>
