<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又能了知諸法實相的智慧應該也成為毫無作用。若一切都是過去世決定，雜染便會一直雜染，無法轉染成淨；智慧也都是過去形成的，則過去邪見現在也是邪見，不可能有正見出現，所以有智慧的行者透過觀察了知我應該轉捨雜染，我應該成就無分別智來斷除雜染，成就清淨聖道的智慧，這件事也沒有作用了。如此，便有毀謗正智的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6768"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此我應轉等者：轉謂轉捨，了知染已，此應轉故。成謂成就，了知淨已，此應成故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中的「轉」是指轉捨，了知煩惱雜染、業雜染、生雜染是應該要棄捨轉變的。「成」是指成就，了知聖道是清淨的應該要成就。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼非有故，此亦非有，故如實智理不成就。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「彼」是指轉捨雜染，若一切都是過去世決定，雜染便會一直雜染，轉染成淨這件事是不可得的，所以說「非有」；「此」是指如實智理，轉染成淨這件事既然不可得，如實通達實相的智慧必定也無法成就，因為一切全都已被決定了。故依宿因論等的理論在道理上來說，便有毀謗正智的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、出過</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出過，說明外道的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">智不成故，念不安住；念不住故，無三摩地；無有定故，不正尋思，令心迷亂；心迷亂故，便應欣慕愚夫同意所樂諸根；由彼獲得愚夫同意所樂法故，是則退失并沙門法及沙門論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種過失是毀謗正智的過失。由於所主張的宿因論、無因論都是錯誤的，若一切都已被過去所作或主宰者決定，如實智不能成就故，正念便不能安住；正念不能安住的緣故，無法得三摩地；未得定的緣故，會導致不正尋思，使令心迷惑障亂；心識迷亂的緣故，便會欣仰羡慕，同意愚夫以享受欲樂為最上等的想法；由於認同愚夫以享受欲樂為第一的緣故，便會退失聖道，不能成就聖道的法門，也不能成就沙門的正論。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　宿因論等認為既然一切都已被決定，無法改變，精進也沒有用，還不如痛快一點過活，好好享受當下的欲樂；由於有這樣的觀念，無法成就聖道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名為第三過失。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是名為第三過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼非有故等者：謂彼現在士用若許非有，此如實智亦應非有故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果認為現在人為的努力是沒有作用的，則轉染成淨不可得，如實的正智便也應不可能成就，這是邪因論的過失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、攝略說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科攝略說，重新將惡因論的過失要略歸納成三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若略說此，有三種過。謂現在世諸不善受因不成過、謗精進過、謗正智過。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若要略說惡因論與無因論，有三種過失：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、現在世諸不善受因不成過。將現在世造不善業而有樂受的因，推託全都是由過去的宿業所作，或是他化自在天所變，或是無因而有，這種惡因論與無因論都不能成立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、謗精進過。若認為一切都是宿因所作，已經決定了，即使精進也沒有用，會有毀謗精進的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、謗正智過。既然一切都已決定，無法轉染成淨，則也無法成就正智，所以有謗正智過。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、成不雜染3　申一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成不雜染，說明什麼才是成就無有雜染的正確業果理論，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6769"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何施設領受一切業異熟論，由五種相成不雜染？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何由五種相正確施設領受一切業異熟論，成就不雜染？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來五種相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂若能領受者，若由此領受，若如是領受，若領受時如是雜染、如是清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五種相是指：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、若能領受者，指五取蘊，五蘊能領受業果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、若由此領受，指六觸處，由六根接觸六境可以領受業果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、若如是領受，說明如何領受業果。由名色、六入、觸、受次第領受業果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、若領受時如是雜染，領受時生起雜染。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、若領受時如是清淨，領受時生起清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應該由這五種相貌的說明，使令施設造業得果的理論圓滿正確。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋4　酉一、能領受者</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋這五相，分四科；第一科能領受者，說明能領受業果是五取蘊。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，依五取蘊，施設假名補特伽羅為領受者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　誰在領受這些業果？應當知道此處文中，是依所得到有漏的色受想行識五蘊，假名安立有情是果報領受者。取是煩惱，由取得此五蘊，故名五取蘊。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由此領受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由此領受，說明由六觸處領受業果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此假者，由六觸處故能領受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　即依此假名安立的有情，由六根六塵六識和合生起六觸而有六受，故能領受各種苦、樂、不苦不樂的果報。「由此領受」的「此」是指六觸處，有情藉由六觸處領受業果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、如是領受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科如是領受，說明領受果報的過程。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於母胎中四種差別，謂依精血大種所造，諸業、煩惱之所攝受，結生相續有取之識，及母腹中所有孔穴。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於入母胎中有四種胎位差別，即下文所說名色、六處、觸、受。受生有情於中有滅的同時，經由母腹中所有孔穴，於是處中有悶絕而受生，由一切種子識（阿賴耶識）的功能勢力，依父精母血與四大種所造和合依託聚集而生，識入母胎，成為煩惱與業所攝受的有取之識。「有取」即是煩惱，第八識中有很多的業、煩惱種子；由業種子使令結生相續，煩惱種子和合苦，將苦與生命結合在一起，得了一個苦的果報，繼續相續下一期的生老病死苦。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6770"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於母胎中四種差別等者：謂如下說：次有名色，次有六處，次觸，次受。是名於母胎中四種差別。於入胎時，父母精血為所依止，名依精血大種所造。中有趣生，業、煩惱力為其增上，由是此說諸業、煩惱之所攝受。餘文易知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於母胎中四種差別，是指下文所說識入母胎的四種位次：一開始是名色，父精母血成就名色，識緣名色，接著有六處，大約七八個星期開始有六根長成，在母胎中也會有觸，有福報的人感受是在宮廷中，薄福的人則覺得是躲在破草屋裡，觸受從在母胎時即有。聲聞乘的道理，觸受是在胎外，而大乘主張觸受在胎裡胎外都有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一開始入胎時，隨業識是依托父精母血和合才能入胎受生，名依精血大種所造。中有趣向生處入胎而受生，是由業、煩惱力為其增上緣，所以文中說「諸業、煩惱之所攝受」。其餘的文容易了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由如是故，得入母胎；次有名色，次有六處，次觸，次受。如是次第而有領受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於上述如是因緣，識得入母胎；其次有名色漸漸滋長，次有六根出現，出胎以後有觸，觸對境界以後有感受。如是依這樣的次第而領受業果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、領受時雜染清淨2　戌一、總標二因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科領受時雜染清淨，說明領受業果時，由如理或不如理作意而生起雜染或清淨，分二科；第一科總標二因，總相標出領受業果的二種因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即此受，亦用現在觸為其因，亦用宿世業等為因。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有情從一入胎乃至一期生命的結束，會領受各式各樣不同的境界，這種感覺領受有此現在的觸為因，也有以過去的業力為因，即依現在及過去這二種因緣，而有諸受，不能說一切都是以過去為因，也不能說一切以現在所作為因。宿因與現緣都有影響，這才是正論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、別顯染淨2　亥一、雜染攝2　天一、出因緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二別顯染淨，各別說明領受業果時生起雜染或清淨的情況，分二科；第一科雜染攝，雜染所攝受，又分二科；第一科出因緣，說出生起雜染的因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼若聽聞諸不正法、非理作意以為因緣，便觸無明觸所生受；受為緣故，復生於愛；愛為緣故，復生於取；乃至當來生老死等眾苦差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情出生以後，如果親近不善士、聽聞不正法，以不如理作意為因緣，不知道我空法空的真理，觸對境界時便生無明相應觸所生受；以此無明觸所生受為緣，又引生愛煩惱；愛煩惱為緣故又會生取，取著種種的境界而造業；乃至感得當來生老死等眾苦差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、明所攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明所攝，說明雜染所攝苦集二諦。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是領受諸無明觸所生受時，便有雜染所攝二諦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是這樣的凡夫在六根接觸六境領受無明觸所生受時，無有我空法空的智慧，必定有煩惱流漏而造業，如此便有雜染所攝的苦、集二諦。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》便有雜染所攝二諦者：此說二諦，謂苦、集諦應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說的二諦，是指苦諦與集諦應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、清淨攝2　天一、出因緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科清淨攝，說明領受業果時清淨所攝受，分二科；第一科出因緣，說出生起清淨的因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">與此相違，聽聞正法、如理作意為因緣故，便能領受明觸所生諸受差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與上述雜染因緣相反，有情受生以後如果能夠親近善士、聽聞正法，以佛所說教法如理作意為因緣，在觸對境界時，便能有明相應觸所生諸受差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　明是指智慧，能知道我空、法空的道理，五蘊諸行乃至生老病死法都不是真實的，我也不是真實的，法也不是真實的。每一次的觸受皆是再次驗證我法二空真如理，時時這樣保持如理作意，便能成就清淨聖道，斷除三界苦果。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6771"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、明所攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明所攝，說明清淨所攝滅道二諦。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受此受時，便有清淨所攝二諦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是這樣的有情在六根接觸六境領受明相應觸所生受時，因有我空法空的智慧，便能成就清淨所攝的滅諦與道諦。這裡說的明相應觸，主要是指無漏慧相應觸。而佛法裡的凡夫，聽聞正法，能夠如理作意，雖然還未成就無漏，也是趣向清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》便有清淨所攝二諦者：此說二諦，謂滅、道諦應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說的二諦，是指滅諦與道諦應該了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、施設業行過患勝利2　午一、過患攝2　未一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科施設業行過患勝利，說明所施設的業行言論有正與邪，邪論有過患，正論則有勝利，分二科；第一科過患攝，說明外道邪論的過患，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二種過患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當知施設邪業清淨及邪行中，有二過患。何等為二？一、內證稽留過患，二、他所譏毀過患。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當了知外道以名言施設邪業清淨及邪行的言論中，有二種過患，是哪二種？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內證稽留過患。本來可以成就聖道，卻因為聽聞不正法，被這些邪論所障礙稽留，因此不能夠得到真實內證的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所譏毀過患。執著邪論是清淨的，但看不到清淨的相貌，便會被他人嘲笑毀謗。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨釋3　申一、施設邪業清淨2　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分三科；第一科施設邪業清淨，說明外道如何施設安立邪業清淨，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何施設邪業清淨？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道如何以名言安立邪業是清淨的？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、出彼論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出彼論，說明他們的理論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂如有一，實非大師，妄分別已，自稱大師。宣說如是邪施設論，謂現法中諸所受苦，一切皆是宿因所作。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一類外道，實際上並不是佛，卻虛妄分別，妄自稱為大師。宣說這樣的邪施設論，主張現在生命體當中所有的苦受，一切都是由過去的業為因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、明彼見3　亥一、舉二因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼見，說明外道的思想，分三科；第一科舉二因，舉出今生所造不善業與所受的二種因。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6772"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼見宿世諸不善業為二種因，謂現法中諸不善業，皆是宿業串習所引；諸所受苦，亦是彼業之所造作。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道觀察過去生的不善業為二種現世因，主張今生所造諸不善業，皆是由於過去串習不善業所引起；今生所受的苦，也都是由於過去所造作的業而來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、成方便2　天一、由修苦行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成方便，外道理論所成就的修行方便，分二科；第一科由修苦行，由修苦行方面說明外道的方便。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由是因緣，修自苦行，令故惡業所招苦果皆悉變吐，更不造作當不善業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道主張現在的苦受是由於過去的業，現在的不善業也都是過去生的宿業所引發，由這種因緣，主張要修自苦行，因為苦受是由過去世的因，如果現在將苦受完，以後便不用再受苦了，依這種理論修苦行，讓自己很痛苦，受很多的苦惱，只要不再造作未來的不善業，便能夠斷除過去惡因所招的苦果。這是外道主張修苦行的邪見，反之佛法說無義苦行當遠離。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、由能防護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由能防護，由能防護方面（持禁戒）說明外道的方便。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於現法中，又能防護身語意住，後當勤修一向善業，令不善法轉成非漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道在現在的生命體當中，有很多的戒禁取規矩，如：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身護方面，要獨居閑靜，都無所見而修苦行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　語護方面，為了避免造惡業，要一生止語；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意護方面，內心要能住於忍受此自逼切苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如此使令身口意不造作不善業，修苦行，待等苦全部都吐掉，將來再一向勤修善業，使令不善法都轉為無漏。這是外道所施設的邪論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、顯究竟</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯究竟，說明苦行外道所主張的究竟。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此因緣，不善業盡；由彼盡故，眾苦亦盡，證苦邊際。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於修苦行的因緣，又能夠防護身語意住，使不善業能盡除；不善業斷盡，苦惱也就盡，可以證得苦邊際。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道並沒有提到煩惱的問題，認為從身業語業下手可以證苦邊際，其實是不能究竟的，因為不知道苦因來自於煩惱、無明，沒有斷煩惱，所以不能究竟清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、邪行3　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科邪行，說明施設邪行的相貌，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何邪行？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是邪行？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、信非真實</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋邪行的體相，分二科；第一科信非真實，所信並非真實。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂如有一，不能了知自業雜染，不能了知彼業對治，又於前後所證差別不如實知。彼成如是愚癡法故，於其師所得無根信，於非信處妄生真實聖教勝解。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　譬如有一類外道的徒眾，不能了解自己所造的業雜染來自哪裡，也不知道如何對治這些業雜染。對於凡夫與聖人所證的境界，如初果二果三果四果，或初禪二禪三禪的差別都不了解。這種人是很愚痴的，不知道戒定慧的次第、染淨的相貌、凡聖的相貌，在外道老師之處得到沒有善根的迷信，沒有根據的信仰，只是聽老師這樣說，好像有一番道理，而自身又沒有智慧可以去分別，相信的不是真實的聖教，在不應產生信心處生起信心，虛妄的以為是真實聖教的勝解。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6773"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、疑不決了2　亥一、由不請問</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科疑不決了，疑惑不能解決，分二科；第一科由不請問，由不請問善知識故疑不能決了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由墜墮非實非理，邪論朋黨他迴動時，於可疑處而不生疑，不尋求師躬往請問：為能正記，為不能記？為能淨疑，為不能淨？為一切智、非一切智？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　相信外道的有情墮落到不是真實聖教處，不是如理作意的處所，不了解真實義，而這些邪論朋黨被他人論破，迴轉改口時，於應該可以懷疑的地方不去懷疑，也不去向真實的善知識恭敬請問自己所親近者：是能正確的記別，或不能記別？能清除自己的疑惑，或者不能？所請問的對象是一切智者、或不是一切智者？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、由畢竟轉3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由畢竟轉，由於大師去世，疑惑畢竟還是會再生起，不能決了，分三科；第一科標，標示出疑惑畢竟生起的原因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大師去世，於所疑處畢竟隨轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於佛已經逝世，找不到善知識，內心的問題沒有人可以釋疑，因此疑惑也就一直存在。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋善知識的重要。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大師住世，能為決了此一切智、非一切智。大師滅後，何所請問？云何決了？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛在世時，才能決定某人是否具足正見，是一切智者，或不是一切智者。佛已滅度後，哪裡還有善知識可以請問呢？如何能毫無疑問地決斷邪正？由於外道認為佛已去世，無處請法，因此疑惑恆常相續。外道不知道佛有留下很多教法，如果能深入經藏就有決擇判斷的智慧力。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名邪行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類人由於不能自知自業雜染、業的對治、前後所證業果染淨差別，於法有愚癡故，於其師所得無根信，於業果的道理缺乏正確的認知，心懷疑惑，不能決定邪正，是名邪行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能為決了此一切智等者：謂能決了所可疑處，此邪論師為一切智、非一切智故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這種人心裡這樣想，佛已逝世，只有佛可以決了所疑問題，這邪論師到底是一切智者或不是一切智者。又這類人也有高慢心，不肯多請問其他人，現在所跟從學習的人到底是對還是錯？也不容易相信他人所說，因此疑惑一直存在心中。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6774"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、二種過患2　酉一、內證稽留過患3　戌一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科二種過患，施設邪行有二種過患，分二科；第一科內證稽留患，說明由於錯誤認知不能內證涅槃的過患，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何緣應知，如是施設令業清淨，不應道理？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以何種因緣可以了知，外道如是施設苦行是宿因所作，主張苦行可以盡除宿不善業，令業清淨，這樣的主張是不合道理的？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋2　亥一、出不應理2　天一、標列二緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出不應理，說出不合理的理由，分二科；第一科標列二緣，標示列出二緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由二緣故，謂彼苦行宿因所作不應理故，由此能盡宿不善業不應理故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由二種原因證明對方所安立的是錯的：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、外道認為現在的苦行等一切業都是由於宿因所作，這是不合道理的；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、外道主張修苦行可以將過去的不善業都盡除，這也不合道理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋其所以2　地一、苦非宿作</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋其所以，解釋不合道理的原因，分二科；第一科苦非宿作，說明苦行並不是宿業所作。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？軟中上品自苦行緣所逼切時，軟中上品苦受生故；即此三品逼緣遠離，由所逼切三品苦受不得生故；宿因所作不應道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為何外道主張苦行是宿業所作，不合道理？外道為求解脫、或達到某種願望所採取折磨自己的修行方式，名為苦行。隨著軟中上品不同程度的苦行逼迫折磨為緣，各別會有軟中上品的苦受生起。軟是較輕微的苦受，中是中等程度的苦受，上則是很強大的苦受。若遠離這三種品類的苦行，則不生三種苦受；因此若說苦行都是宿因所作，是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、不盡宿業</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不盡宿業，說明苦行不能斷盡過去惡業的原因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此苦行，無有功能令宿所作能感苦受諸不善業成順樂受，是故彼起如是定見，由自苦行，令宿所作惡業變吐，不應道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又，今生的苦果（苦受）是由過去不善業所招感，藉由外道所修的苦行，並無功能使令今生的苦果轉變成順樂受業的樂果，因此外道認為修苦行能將過去所造的惡業轉變吐除，這種定見，是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、別廣徵詰2　天一、詰宿所作2　地一、總徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別廣徵詰，依上述二緣，各別詳細的提出問難，分二科；第一科詰宿所作，即上述所說的第一緣，詰問外道：以苦行為緣所生的苦受是否也為宿業所作，分二科；第一科總徵，總問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有是事，彼宿所作能順苦受諸不善業，為能感得於現法中自苦逼切苦受果不？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　論主提出問題來難問對方：若的確有些事，是由於自己過去所造的，能順苦受的不善業，那麼這往昔的惡業，能感得現在自己修苦行而生的苦受嗎？簡而言之，今生苦行的苦受是否也為宿昔惡業的果報？</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6775"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、別詰2　玄一、詰能感得2　黃一、自然變吐難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地二別詰，分別詰問，依對方不同的執著再各別難問，分二科；第一科詰能感得，難問認為「過去惡業能感得現在苦行的苦受果」者，其中再以自然變吐及後果非吐來難問對方：「苦行所作的苦受是否為宿業所感的果」，又分二科；第一科自然變吐難，自然變吐的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若言感得此苦受果，修自苦行即為唐捐。受彼果已，自然變吐。若如是者，宿世所作諸不善業，非自苦行所能變吐。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果認為過去能順苦受的不善業能感得現在此苦受的果，代表苦受的果報是由過去順苦受的不善業所招感的，則現在修的苦行即是白費了。因為，過去造的惡業由於因緣成熟而感得果報，業因已受用便不會再感果，苦果自然也沒有了。若是這樣，過去所作的諸不善業也不是自作苦行所能變吐的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、後果非吐難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後果非吐難，後果非吐的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即此業一分可吐。謂現法中受彼果者，若餘能順後所受業，彼於後世當受其果，非自苦行可令其果悉皆變吐。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又即此宿世所作諸不善業，有順生受、順後受，只有順生受這一分受果之後，可自然變吐，其餘順後受業，必須下一生以後才受其果，並非今生苦行可以斷除。因此外道認為現在修苦行能將過去曾造的惡業完全變吐、斷除，是不合道理的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、詰非感得</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科詰非感得，難問認為「逼切苦受不是宿因所感得」者，如果對方說不是宿業所感得，也不合道理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若言現在逼切苦受非宿因作，如是所說諸所領受，一切皆是宿因所作，不應道理。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果外道說現在逼迫的苦受不是過去不善業所造的，如此一來自己所主張的所有領受都是宿業所作，便會前後不一致，不合道理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、詰盡宿業3　地一、出業決定2　玄一、別辨相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科詰盡宿業，即上述所說的第二緣，要難問對方修外道的苦行能否將過去的業都斷除？事實上這是不可能的，分三科；第一科出業決定，說出由定業決定，又分二科；第一科別辨相，各別說明相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如能隨順苦受惡業，不可令其成順樂受；如是宿世所作能順樂受善業，不可令其成順不苦不樂受業。或彼二種順現法受，不可令其成順後受；若順後受，不可令其成無所受。若未成熟，不可令熟；若已成熟，不可彼彼方便令轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果之前造的業是順苦受的惡業，透過苦行不可能改變它成順樂受；同樣，過去生所造能感今生順樂受的善業，透過苦行也無法使令它變成順不苦不樂受的業，苦行沒有這樣的功能。或者由宿世善、惡二業所感的二種順現法受（苦受、樂受），若想透過苦行令其轉成順後受，這也是不可得的；若過去造的業，透過苦行也無法使令它成無所受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若業還沒有成熟，修苦行也無法使令成熟；如果已成熟，不可能用不同方式的苦行，使令它轉變。例如過去積欠了別人十元，只是一直獨自的作金雞獨立等苦行，是無法還清欠款的，因為二者並不相關。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6776"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或彼二種順現法受者：此說二種，即善、惡業應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文所說的二種順現法受，即是過去所造善、惡業相應的苦受、樂受，應能了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、攝要義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科攝要義，將前文所說的統攝出要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中所說要略義者，所謂一切善不善業，自性決定、時分決定、品類決定。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上述文中所說的要略義理，是指一切善、不善業，它的自性是決定的；有的時間已決定，是定業，或不定業，假如是定業又有許多種，或是順生受、或順後受、或順現受；此外，品類也是決定的，是順現受的樂受相應，或是苦受相應等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此佛說無義的苦行當遠離。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、詰無堪能2　玄一、隨業決定難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科詰無堪能，第二緣的第二個別問，難問無堪能來說，分二科；第一科隨業決定難，隨業決定的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若如是者，隨業決定，必能攝受如是類果。於中更自受逼切苦，復何所用。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若過去造下的是順苦受的不善業，當然就有順苦受出現，能成就屬於這一種類的果。即使現在加上苦行，自己逼迫自己來受苦，也只是徒增上去的，不能斷除過去業所攝受的苦果。由於過去造的業，會得什麼果已經決定，因此修外道的苦行不能將它斷除，這是沒有用的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、隨自所許難</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨自所許難，隨自所承許的難問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又若此受宿業因感，彼自所許令業一分滅盡可得少分勝利。由是因緣，如此所計少分勝利亦無所有。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如果現在的苦受是由過去的不善業所感得的，彼外道自己承許，由修苦行可以斷除部分的業，得到少分的利益，轉苦受成樂受。然而以修苦行為緣能生起苦受，由此苦行的因緣，只是苦上加苦，連所計著的少分勝利也不可得。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、結終無脫</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結終無脫，前二緣的結說，可知透過這樣的苦行終究無法解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是則為極自稽留業所縛故，終無解脫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說則知，外道自認為要修苦行以斷業，其實只是用苦行將自己稽留在其中：被自己苦行所作的，極為障礙涅槃，稽留生死苦的業所繫縛，最終仍然無法解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此道理，是名於此邪論邪行第一過患，謂於內證自義稽留。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此道理，是名於此邪論邪行的第一個於內證自義稽留的過患。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道說修苦行能夠斷除宿業，然而對於自己成就涅槃的義利只是一種障礙，將自己稽留在凡夫的境界，根本無法解脫清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6777"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、他所譏毀過患2　戌一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科他所譏毀過患，說明邪論邪行的第二個過患：其他人看到這類人修苦行並沒有快樂的果報，也會譏嫌、毀謗，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何他所譏毀過患？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是其他有情譏諷、毀謗的過患？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋2　亥一、出彼論行2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出彼論行，說出對方的邪論、苦行，又分二科；第一科標，標示出依二種邪論能起三種苦行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼依止二種邪論，發起三種自苦惱行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道依止這二種惡因的邪論，發起三種自苦惱行。（註：前面「未一、成雜染」那一科中，說有惡因論及無因論，然此處只說二種惡因論。）</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋2　地一、二種邪論2　玄一、第一邪論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科二種邪論，說明二種邪論，又分二科；第一科第一邪論，說明第一種邪論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是說：所有士夫補特伽羅，諸所領受，一切皆是宿因所作。是名第一邪論，謂惡因論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道主張：所有的人，所領受的一切都是過去業所造的，這是名第一邪論。這是惡因論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、第二邪論</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種第二邪論，說明第二邪論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有說言：如彼最初自在變化，從是已後，諸所領受，一切皆是宿業所作。是名第二邪論，謂惡因論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有外道主張：最初投生時，是由大自在天所變化的，從此以後，所有領受到的苦、樂、不苦不樂受都是過去造業所感，是名第二邪論。這也是惡因論。由此而發動三種苦行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、三自苦行2　玄一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科三自苦行，說明三種自苦行，分二科；第一科標，標出即身語意三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三種自苦行者，謂身語意護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三種自苦行方面，即身護、語護、及意護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋3　黃一、身護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；分三科；第一科身護，說明外道主張的身護。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6778"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身護者，謂不以身與餘有情共相雜住，唯往山林、阿練若處，獨居閑靜，都無所見而修苦行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道的身護方面，即不以自身與其餘有情雜住。外道的邪知邪見認為修行不能跟其他人共住在一起，應到山林、寂靜的精舍中，一人獨住以求閑靜，並且要隔絕外緣的接觸，都無所見而修苦行。這是第一種自苦行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、語護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科語護，說明外道主張的語護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">語護者，謂彼受持默無言禁。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道的語護方面，即是受持不說話的戒，盡形壽都不說話，因為怕造業所以不說話，一生止語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、意護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科意護，說明外道主張的意護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">意護者，謂心忍受自逼切苦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道的意護方面，是主張內心要能忍耐自己逼迫自己所產生的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是外道苦行的三種相貌。自討苦吃還逼迫自己要忍耐。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、顯他譏毀2　天一、出其因緣2　地一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯他譏毀，顯示他人的譏毀，分二科；第一科出其因緣，說明其中緣因，又分二科；第一科標，標示出因自苦不能越度而被他人所譏毀的因緣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼起如是欲樂言說，為他顯示，由此二種所見圓滿，及由三種苦行圓滿，能越眾苦。然其自苦不能越度，是故為他之所譏毀。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　彼外道生起這樣欲樂的言說：為其他人等顯示，這二種自認是圓滿的邪見道理，認為由這三種苦行圓滿能夠超越眾苦。然而這種自苦的苦行並不能超越、度脫苦惱，因此被他人譏毀。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸所受一切皆是宿因所作，亦是自在變化因作，亦是三種苦行能越因之所作，是則三種修苦行俱所受眾苦，定是宿世黑業所感，亦是暴惡自在所化，三種苦行皆不能越，是故於今受斯苦受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　倘若如外道主張現在所領受的感覺，皆是過去的業因所作的，也是大自在天變化因所作，也是身語意護三種苦行能超越的因所作，則此三種修苦行的苦惱聚在一起所受的苦，一定是過去造的不善業所感得的，也是暴惡自在天（欲界天的魔王）所變化的，然而外道們修這三種苦行都不能超越眾苦，反而引生痛苦，被他人譏毀，因此於現今受到這些苦受。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6779"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、結名過患</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名過患，結說名過患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼雖復內證稽留，而有為他所稱讚者，猶尚不可，況此為他稱讚勝利亦無所有，是故名為第二過患。由此分故，唯可譏毀。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若外道修這種自認能斷宿業的苦行而稽留在凡夫境界，無法入涅，還能有被他人稱讚的情況，尚且不可以修這種無義的苦行，何況根本沒有人稱讚。這些外道既沒有得到被他人稱讚的殊勝利益，反而招致譏毀，因此是名第二過患。這是由於無義的苦行，只能招人譏毀而已。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、勝利攝2　未一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科勝利攝，由佛法正論所攝的勝利，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，與上相違，當知施設正業染淨及正行中，有二勝利。一者、內證無滯勝利，二者、他所稱讚勝利。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，與上面外道的邪知邪見相反，佛法以名言施設正業相應的雜染與清淨差別及身語意正行中，依教奉行能得二種勝利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內證無滯勝利。能沒有滯礙的內證清淨的無分別智。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所稱讚勝利。由於確實可以轉染成淨，因此成就聖道後能為他人所稱讚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法不像外道修無義的苦行，不但沒有人稱讚，反而被人譏毀。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨釋3　申一、施設正業染淨2　酉一、辨2　戌一、施設業雜染論3　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨著上文的二種利益作解釋，分三科；第一科施設正業染淨，安立內法正業染淨，又分二科；第一科辨，分別，又分二科；第一科施設業雜染論，說明佛所安立的業雜染論，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何施設業雜染論？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼樣施設業雜染論？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有二業。一者、善業，二、不善業。於過去世已曾造作善不善業，今現法中受愛非愛異熟果等。受愛非愛果差別時，更復造作善不善業，由此當來受愛非愛異熟果等。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法說業有二種。一、善業，二、不善業。如果有情在過去世曾經造過善業或不善業，因此有情於現在的生命體中能得到可愛的果報或不可愛的果報。又依止現在的果報繼續造善業或不善業，將來仍舊繼續感得可愛或不可愛的果報。這是正確的說法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語施設業雜染論。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6780"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名為業雜染論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，依善不善業而有異熟果、等流果及增上果等生雜染，依止生雜染又繼續造善、不善業，又有當來的生雜染。如是依於業而有雜染，名業雜染。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除此處外，〈攝事分〉卷88也曾說明過何謂業雜染：「若諸新業、造作增長；若諸故業、數數觸已，而不變吐。是名業雜染。」。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8更曾由自性、分別、因、位、門、上品、顛倒、差別、過患等不同角度來詳細解釋業雜染的內容。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》受愛非愛異熟果等者：此中等言，等取餘等流果及增上果應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上文「受愛非愛異熟果等」中的等字，包括其餘的等流果、及增上果應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如《顯揚聖教論》卷1所云：「業雜染者：謂或因煩惱所生，或因煩惱緣助善法所生。如其所應，三界所攝身業語業意業，此復二種。一、思，二、思所起。此業差別，復有多種。欲界所攝，名福非福。色無色界所攝，名為不動。復有引業。謂作及增長，能引種種有情世間及器世間果及異熟。復有生業。謂前所引，助令生故。」也可配合此處作理解。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、施設業清淨論3　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科施設業清淨論，說明佛所安立的業清淨論，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何施設業清淨論？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法如何安立業的清淨論？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂如有一，不造新業，故業觸已，尋復變吐，由對治力永斷無餘，故得清淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　譬如有一類人，不再造作新的業，雖然由過去的業因，現在現行由觸、受已得到了果報，但由聖道的對治力，將煩惱種子永斷無餘，不再造業，因此業得以清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語施設業清淨論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名為令雜染業得清淨論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是佛法中所說的：透過聖道對治煩惱，使令業得到清淨，是名為令雜染業得清淨論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語施設正業染淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是施設正業染淨，名無上論。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛這樣以語言來安立正業的雜染論或業的清淨論，是與正見相應的無上論，世間其它理論沒有能超越佛法這種真實的理論。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、正行3　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科正行，聞思修正行，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何正行？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法所說的正行是什麼？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、由聞思</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科由聞思，解釋聞思正行。佛法的正行是親近善士、聽聞正法、如理作意、法隨法行。首先要聽聞佛法、思惟佛法是第一個正行。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6781"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂如有一，於正法中成就多聞，於業雜染及以清淨，正知雜染、清淨相已，捨不善業，修習善業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一類人，在正法中成就多聞，對於業雜染及業清淨，正確的了知雜染清淨的相貌，了解以後能棄捨不善業，修習善業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、由修治3　亥一、修習止觀2　天一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由修治，由修習止觀對治諸蓋，遠離眾苦，分三科；第一科修習止觀，說明修習止觀的正行，又分二科；第一科總標，總相標出要義</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於聞思如理作意勤方便已，為證修故，住空閑處，淨修治心，令離諸蓋及眾苦法。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　彼行者由聽聞正法及思惟佛法、如理作意精勤為方便之後，為了證得修所成慧，安住在空閑清淨的處所，修習對治煩惱使心清淨，令心遠離貪欲、瞋恚、惛沈睡眠、掉舉惡作及疑這五種定蓋障，及各種身心苦惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、別釋2　地一、令離諸蓋2　玄一、止所對治</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋離諸蓋及離眾苦法，分二科；第一科令離諸蓋，以止觀使令自己遠離諸蓋，又分二科；第一科止所對治，修止來對治貪欲、瞋恚、掉舉惡作蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲斷除貪欲、瞋恚、掉舉惡作，以九種行安住其心，令心棄捨止所對治。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修止時，為了斷除貪欲蓋、瞋恚蓋、掉舉惡作蓋，以九心住──內住、等住、安住、近住、調順、寂靜、最極寂靜、專住一趣、等持，安住其心，令心棄捨於修習止品所要對治的貪欲等蓋的掉動，不惛沉，不散亂，於所緣境，明靜而住。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以九種行安住其心者：聲聞地說九種心住，其相應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/30.htm#68700:25203">陵本三十卷九頁2511</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷30，1005頁曾說過九心住的相貌，查閱該處即可了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、觀所對治</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科觀所對治，第二科修觀來對治惛沈睡眠蓋、疑蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲斷除惛沈睡眠及以疑蓋，分析六事如理作意，修飾其心，令心棄捨觀所對治。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修觀行時，為了斷除惛沈睡眠及疑蓋，分析所緣境的義、事、相、品、時、理六事差別所緣，依文思惟觀察如理作意，修治調伏內心，使令內心能夠棄捨觀品所要對治的惛沈睡眠及疑。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》分析六事者：聲聞地說六事差別所緣毗鉢舍那，其相應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/30.htm#68703:25303">陵本三十卷十二頁2520</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六種事是義、事、相、品、時、理 。為了斷除惛沈睡眠及疑蓋，在尋思所緣境時，應思惟六件事，以不淨所緣為例：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、尋思義，義是道理；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、尋思事，尋思所依法體的事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、尋思相，思惟所緣的自相、共相；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、尋思它的品類，功過稱為品類，若是黑品有過失，白品則有功德；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、尋思時，尋思所緣於過去、現在、未來時間上的相貌；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、尋思理，依觀待道理、作用道理、證成道理、法爾道理，四種道理尋思所緣境。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　每一種所緣都有這六種角度，這些相貌應該知道，在〈聲聞地〉卷30，1008頁裡都已說過。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6782"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、令離眾苦</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科令眾離苦，說明令眾離苦。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從彼止觀所治出已，能正修學，消伏眾苦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者從止觀對治五蓋以後，最先成就的是欲界定的等持，進一步成就未到地定，能夠獲得輕安，接著依此未到地定，其次為成就修慧，於法觀中修增上慧。如此正確數數串習修學止觀，能消除調伏身心各種苦惱，令心清淨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、思擇受用2　天一、總標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科思擇受用，修止觀還要有很多因緣配合，日常生活中受用衣服、飲食、臥具、湯藥，都要有智慧思惟簡擇，才不會被欲所迷惑，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出要義</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼既如是淨修其心，令離諸蓋眾苦法已，復於衣服、飲食、臥具受用儀則，淨修其心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者這樣清淨修習內心，令心遠離諸蓋身心各種苦法，又對於日常生活中受用的衣服、飲食、臥具，以及威儀軌則也要注意，好好的清淨修治這一念心，令心不散亂，離諸貪欲。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、別辨2　地一、受用麤弊</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別分別，分二科；第一科受用麤弊，受用麤弊的資生眾具。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由習近如是衣服乃至臥具，不善法增，善法退減，即便遠離。寧可受用麤弊衣等，惙爾自存，忍受眾苦，進修正行。</span></strong></span></span>
