<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者還要觀察自己，受用衣服飲食臥具時，如果心裡常常貪念歡喜穿上等美服、食用精緻的食物、睡臥豪華的臥具，只是突增自己的欲心，使不善法增長，戒定慧善法退減。為了對治貪欲心，應修遠離法，對於所得到的上好美服可展轉布施供養有德的上座，寧可忍受困劣穿粗布衣裳、食用粗漏能溫飽的飲食、使用邊際臥具，捨棄自己過往的習氣，必需忍受眾苦，捨棄自己煩惱進修正行。惙（音ㄔㄨㄛˋ或音 ㄔㄨㄟˋ）爾自存，忍受困劣受用義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、受用勝妙3　玄一、顯過患2　黃一、標流漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科受用勝妙，受用勝妙衣服等，分三科；第一科顯過患，顯示其中的過患，又分二科；第一科標流漏，標出煩惱流漏的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由二緣，受用勝妙衣服等因，能令生長惡不善法，謂諸妄想不正尋思。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由二種緣，受用勝妙衣物等資生具為因，為計劃如何得到這些物資，種種的妄想不正尋思在腦海中不斷出現，甚至攀緣信徒，走訪富貴人家，以利求利，因而生出、長養種種惡不善法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、釋二緣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋二緣，解釋二種因緣使令惡不善法增長。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等二緣？一、於諸善未能長時串修習故，心不調柔；二、於衣服、飲食等事欲貪堅著。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪二緣？一、沒有長時間串習戒定慧的善法，善法力量不夠，有很多的煩惱，心不調柔，經常為了資生眾具的事起煩惱。二、受用好的資具之後，便不願再受用粗弊的資具，受用的資具愈好，欲貪愈堅固執著。由這二種因緣使令惡不善法增長。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6783"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、明思擇</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明思擇，說明行者如何正確思惟決擇。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由是因緣，修正行者調柔其心，令堪所作；於衣服等欲貪堅著，及諸無常眾緣生法，恆常繫念，深見過患。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行人了知前文所說二種因緣，以修正行調伏自心的煩惱，令心有堪能修聖道。分二點說明：一、長時間串習戒定慧令心調柔，使心有堪能性證得聖道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、對衣服飲食臥具湯藥等欲貪的堅固執著，恆常繫念思惟衣服等事是無常苦法，眾緣生法，無我無我所，深見欲貪的過患，令心遠離。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、結無染</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結無染，結說無有雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時雖復受用勝妙衣服等事，而於其中無有雜染。如是行者亦受安樂，亦無有罪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當行者修學止觀調柔其心後，雖然受用勝妙的衣服、飲食、臥具等事，對於所受用物心無雜染，無欲貪堅著，不會因為受用勝妙的衣服、飲食、臥具而障礙自己的修行。這樣的行者也可以受用勝妙的資具，是沒有罪過的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、通達隨眠3　天一、出為染</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科通達隨眠，通達煩惱種子過患，勤修正行漏盡解脫；分三科；第一科出為染，指出隨眠未斷仍有雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由奢摩他、毗鉢舍那修習力故，淨修其心離諸蓋已，由思擇力，於衣服等邪受用故，雖於爾時暫少成就心一境性，欲貪隨眠仍未斷故，於當來世復為雜染。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者由止、觀的修習力，淨修其心遠離諸蓋後，由於思擇力，對於衣服飲食臥具的欲貪等邪受用能深見過患，雖然成就未到地定，暫時沒有欲貪堅著的現行，但由於欲貪的種子仍未斷除，將來還是在生死中繼續雜染，未來世若有因緣，欲貪仍會起現行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於衣服等邪受用故等者：前說於衣服等欲貪堅著，名邪受用。恆常繫念，深見過患，名於爾時暫少成就心一境性。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對衣服飲食臥具有欲貪堅著，名為邪受用。此時行者若能恆常繫念眾緣生法諸行無常，深見欲貪的過患無窮，勤修止觀，斷除欲貪，便能成就心一境性；雖然能夠成就心一境性，但是煩惱種子並沒有斷，將來還是會繼續雜染，名於爾時暫少成就心一境性。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6784"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、明修斷</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明修斷，說明修斷。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼以妙慧通達是已，便修加行。為畢竟斷，受用如法邊際臥具，離諸貪著，先善修治正定資糧，漸次乃至能入清淨第四靜慮。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者以微妙的智慧觀察、通達種種的邪受用，有種種過患以後，便精進修止修觀。為了畢竟斷除煩惱的種子，在生活上受用如法的邊際臥具，遠離種種的貪著，先栽培正定的二道資糧，漸次能證得初靜慮乃至能入清淨的第四靜慮。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、顯解脫</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯解脫，顯示得到解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">以此為依，證諦現觀，隨得漏盡心善解脫。於一切苦得離繫故，究竟寂靜所攝受故，微妙清淨一切身心無間滿故，一切煩惱永離繫故，普能領納諸無漏受。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者以靜慮為依止，在定中修苦集滅道四諦十六行相的觀行，證得四諦現觀，乃至隨順獲得斷盡煩惱的功德，心善解脫貪瞋癡的繫縛。證得阿羅漢果，得無生智，於三界一切苦果得永離繫故，為究竟寂靜涅槃之所攝受，一切身心無間充滿微妙清淨的覺受，永久遠離三界所有愛見煩惱的繫縛，六根觸對六境，遍於一切諸法，普能領納無漏聖道相應的喜樂捨受。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名正行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法正行首在依聞思建立正見，再修止觀，以奢摩他毗鉢舍那修淨其心，成就少分心一境性，降伏現行的煩惱；以此為基再修加行，善修治正定資糧成就根本定；以此為依止證諦現觀乃至證得漏盡，永離繋伏一切煩惱種子，此為佛法之正行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、二勝利</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科二勝利，佛法施設的正業染淨及正行，可以得到二種殊勝的利益。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是應知內證無滯，及彼相違五種差別他所稱讚。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法所施設的正業染淨及正行，能成就二種殊勝的利益，第一是內證無滯，第二是他所稱讚，與先前所說外道論會有的「內證稽留」與「他所譏毀」二種過患相反。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內證無滯方面，行者依止佛法所施設正業染淨及正行而修行，於證得諦現觀的諸法實相，無有滯礙；外道所主張以修苦行令宿世所造諸惡業清淨的認知反而滯礙證得諦現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他所稱讚方面，佛法沒有外道二種邪論與三種自苦惱行的五種差別，不為他所譏毀，並為其他眾生所稱讚。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》及彼相違五種差別等者：前說他所譏毀過患，謂彼依止二種邪論，發起三種自苦惱行，是名五種差別。今說他所稱讚，與彼相違，應知其相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說到被外人所譏諷毀謗的過患，是外道才有的情況。因為外道有惡因論及無因論的二種邪論，發起身護、語護及意護三種自苦惱行，這樣的苦行並不能得到解脫，因而被他人所譏毀。佛法雖然也有規定身語意業要如何防護，但是佛法主張中道而行，並不一定要苦行，也不主張樂行。生活所需的資生具不論所受用是麤弊或勝妙，只要內心都是清淨不離善法，於受用資具等能深見過患，並不障礙證入現觀，所以佛法所施設的正業染淨及正行確實可以轉染成淨，成就聖道為他人所稱讚，與外道邪行邪論主張相反，應當了知其中的相狀。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6785"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於爾時，從諸蓋纏及一切苦心善解脫，於現法中彼諸隨眠無餘永斷，前際、後際業及異熟所有雜染皆善解脫，由於現法獲得聖道及道果故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者能夠精進的修學，這時從五蓋諸纏種種的煩惱及一切苦中心善解脫出來，在現在的生命體中愛見煩惱的種子沒有剩餘全部斷除，過去生無量劫以來，到未來，所有的業及異熟所有雜染都能善巧斷除而得解脫，由此成就聖道及證得阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、施設補特伽羅差別3　午一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科施設補特伽羅差別，施設修行人的差別，分三科；第一科標，標示出三種人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，略有三種補特伽羅。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，約略歸納起來有三種人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、未入聖教異生，二者、已入聖教有學，三者、已入聖教異生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、還沒有入到佛門中的凡夫；二、已到佛法中，已經修學證得有學的聖人，包括初果乃至四果向；三、已到聖教中來的凡夫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋2　未一、標由三相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋三種人的情況，分二科；第一科標由三相，標出各有三種相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由三種相，應知最初補特伽羅。第二、第三，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道最初及第二、第三種補特伽羅，分別各有三種情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋其差別3　申一、未入聖教異生2　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋其差別，解釋其中的差別，分三科；第一科未入聖教異生，說明未進入聖教的凡夫，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三相，應知最初補特伽羅？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應該了知最初未進入聖教的凡夫，會有哪三種相貌？三相即是有斷非生、有生非斷、及亦斷亦生，下文會再詳細解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋3　戌一、有斷非生2　亥一、標類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科有斷非生，未入聖教凡夫中的第一相是有斷非生，指先已有世間正見，後入外道隨外道而轉，其後又得遇正法以斷除邪見的情況；又分二科；第一科標類，標出未入聖教凡夫中的第一類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂初有一補特伽羅，已得成就世間正見，了知有施，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最初有一類有情，雖然還沒有到佛門，但是已成就世間的正見，於世間有正確的因果觀，了知布施、敬愛、祭祀、供養父母可以得到福報，知道善因樂果、惡因苦果的道理。這類人的知見不是出世見的正見，並沒有無漏的智慧，但是對於因果有正確的觀念，與其他有情或外道毀謗作善事沒有功德的邪見是不一樣的，乃至詳細內容如卷8所說。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6786"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》了知有施乃至廣說者：謂有施與、有愛養、有祠祀，與彼一切誹謗邪見相違，故名正見。有尋有伺地廣說諸邪見相應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#68746:6017">陵本八卷十四頁611</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　卷8說外道誹撥沒有布施恭敬愛養的功德及除了火天以外，沒有值得祭祀的對象。這裡所說第一類有情是有世間正確的因果觀，知道有布施、有愛養、有祠祀，與外道的一切誹謗邪見是相反的，故名正見。在〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷8，252頁中有詳細說種種邪見的體相應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、辨相2　天一、出隨轉</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，分別第一種有斷非生的凡夫，有二種特相，分二科；第一科出隨轉，出離正見隨不正見轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於異時，聞不正法為因緣故，而便發起非理作意。世間正見臨將欲滅，雖未一切悉皆已滅，而堪能滅；又彼所治誹謗邪見臨將欲生，雖未已生，而堪能生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尚未入佛門的凡夫，最初開始有一些世間的正見，對於因果有正確的觀念，知道布施、愛養、祠祀是有功德的。可是之後，聽到不正法的因緣，發起不如理作意，由於不正見不斷不斷的熏習，過去的世間正見雖然沒有全部斷除，但所熏習的不正見有堪能將世間的正見全部滅除；又所應對治毀謗無因無果的邪見由於即將產生，雖然猶未生起，然而有堪能生，可能會隨外道所說沒有愛養祠祀的邪知邪見而轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、明斷生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明斷生，正式說明凡夫有斷非生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於中間，聽聞正法為因緣故，遂還發生如理作意。彼臨欲生誹謗邪見不現行故，說名為斷；然其正見先成就故，不名為生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此未入聖教的凡夫，由於常熏習不正見因緣，思想將要變成邪見，後來又有因緣聽到正法，能夠如理作意而摒棄邪見，斷除邪見名「有斷」。非生是這種人本來有世間正見，後來學習正法更加明白因果道理，雖能如理作意而摒棄邪見，因其已先成就了世間的正見，已有因果觀，所以不能稱為生，名為「非生」。這是第一種人的狀態，是有斷非生的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、有生非斷</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有生非斷，說明未入聖教凡夫的第二種相貌，由於聽聞正法而生起世間正見，本來沒有邪見，所以也不需要斷除邪見。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二，有一補特伽羅，不成正見及以邪見，聽聞正法、如理作意為因緣故，爾乃發生世間正見。彼於邪見不名為斷，先不成故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種凡夫在未接觸佛法之前，沒有世間的正見，但也沒有邪見，後來聽聞到佛法，能如理作意，栽培正確的世間因果觀，令世間的正見產生，是為「有生」。因為本身並沒有邪見，所以沒有斷不斷的問題，不名為「非斷」。這是第二種人的狀態，是有生非斷的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、亦斷亦生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科亦斷亦生，斷了邪見，而後聽聞正法，又生起世間正見。這是未入聖教凡夫的第三相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6787"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三，有一補特伽羅，成就邪見，聽聞正法、如理作意為因緣故，斷滅邪見，生起正見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三是屬外道的有情，先有邪見，後來聽聞到佛法、如理作意為因緣，將錯誤的邪見斷除，是名「亦斷」，又生起正見，是名「亦生」，因此第三種人，屬亦斷亦生的種類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、已入聖教有學2　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科已入聖教有學，說明已入佛門的有學聖人，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三相，應知第二補特伽羅？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道，如何由三種相了知第二類已入聖教的有學聖人？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、標類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標類，標出有學聖者的第一類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於佛等已得證淨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已入聖道證得初果乃至四果向的聖人，以無漏智如實覺知四聖諦理，故這類有情的共通性為對佛、法、僧、戒四種已經得到證淨，內心成就堅固不壞之淨信，不再被外人所轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨相3　亥一、有生非斷</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，分別三種相，分三科；第一科有生非斷，第一種相貌是有生非斷，說明初果聖人有生非斷的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於佛等先所現起一切無智，當於諸諦得現觀時先已斷盡，是故於今不名為斷；而於佛等證淨俱行明現前故，說名為生。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者還在凡位時原先對於佛法僧戒所現起的一切無智，在證入現觀見道十五心（無礙道）時已斷盡，所以於今解脫道位不名為斷，這是解釋「非斷」；行者於見道第十六心證得初果時，於佛法僧戒的四證淨自然現起俱行，無漏的智慧現前，說名為生，這是解釋「有生」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、有斷非生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有斷非生，第二種相貌說明二果三果聖人有斷非生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即以學道斷修所斷餘品無明，而於其明不名生起，此道與先種類同故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　證初果時，已斷除三界112種分別起的見所斷煩惱，仍然還有所餘十六種俱生起的修所斷無明煩惱品在修道位要斷除，是故名為「有斷」。在二果三果階段，所生起的無漏無分別智不能名為生，因為這類聖道智慧與先前成就初果時，都是同一種類的無分別智，所以名為「非生」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、亦斷亦生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科亦斷亦生，第三種相貌說明四果向聖人證得金剛喻定時亦斷亦生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼無學道將現在前，修斷無明皆悉滅盡，又能生起諸無學明。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四果向聖者無學道即將現前，所證得的金剛喻定能全部斷除修所斷的俱生起無明煩惱，包括將最後一念非想非非想處定的定愛無明斷除，故名為「亦斷」。斷盡煩惱下一剎那即能生起無學的智慧，證得阿羅漢果，故名為「亦生」，因此名為是亦斷亦生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是已入聖教有學的三種相貌，第一相是指有生非斷的初果聖人，第二相是指有斷非生的二果三果聖人，第三相是指亦斷亦生的四果向聖人，這是已入聖教的有學三類人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、已入聖教異生2　酉一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科已入聖教的異生，說明已入佛法的凡夫，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="89p6788"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三相，應知第三補特伽羅？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道，如何由三種相了知第三類已入佛法的凡夫？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、標類</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標類，標出已入聖教異生的第一類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂聞無我相應正法。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是指來到佛門之中，聽聞與無我相應正法的凡夫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨相3　亥一、有斷非生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，分別三種相，分三科；第一科有斷非生，第一種相貌是有斷非生，說明資糧位行者有斷非生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初但由聞發生信解，而未悟入。彼於無我生信解故，能斷我見；未悟入故，不得名為生無我見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最初這類資糧位行者只是經由聽聞佛法而生出對佛法的信心及勝解，可是還未悟入無我的道理。由於行者對無我的道理已深信理解，能將執著五蘊為我的無知斷除，是故名為「有斷」；但是由於只是仰信未真實悟入故，一切時處見聞覺知，還是無法真實與無我見相應，尚未有道力斷除煩惱，不能生無我見，是故名為「非生」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、有生非斷</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種有生非斷，第二種相貌是有生非斷，說明加行位行者有生非斷的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如所聞法，復能如理正思惟時，於無我理能悟入故，乃得名為生無我見，於彼隨眠而未能斷。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　加行位行者程度比較高，進入修慧的階段，在未到地定裡修毗鉢舍那，依著所聽聞的佛法，又能夠深入的如理作意正思惟，於無我道理能悟入的緣故，有能力調伏現行煩惱，可以說這類人生起無我的世間正見，名為「有生」；然而行者的我見種子尚未斷除，仍屬加行位的凡夫，是故名為「未斷」。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、亦斷亦生</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科亦斷亦生，說明加行位以後行者亦斷亦生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此已後，由修道力，證諦現觀，方斷隨眠，發生無漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種行者相貌是亦斷亦生，說明加行位以後行者的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從加行位以後，由修道力繼續修行，修四念處三十七道品，證得聖諦現觀，這時才能斷除我見的種子，成就無漏的智慧，轉凡成聖。行者進入見道位有十六心，下一剎那證入初果，可以稱為亦斷亦生。由於斷除我見的種子，生出無漏的正見，所生的正見與前面的無我見是不同的，此時是無漏相應的出世正見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是施設補特伽羅差別，特別將三類人各分成三種相狀，說明有情正見邪見的差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第八十九</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</form>
